# GPU вҖ” hexa-lang's NVPTX-first GPU substrate (domain SSOT)

> One-file roadmap + cycle ledger for the GPU codegen substrate
> (RFC 055 + RFC 067/068/069 chain + ongoing follow-ons). Domain
> SSOT per `AGENTS.tape` `@D g_plan_consolidation`: cycle-by-cycle
> progression appended to `compiler/PLAN.md`; this file is the
> *forward-looking checklist* + *brainstorm-to-exhaustion roadmap*.

**hexa-lang North-Star в‘  (NN stack)** + **В§12 P4+ chain** + **GOAL вҖ” "cuBLAS-using stacks лҘј whole-program-fusion мңјлЎң мҡ°нҡҢ"** are the umbrella metrics this file tracks.

---

## 0 В· One-paragraph state (end-of-day 2026-05-20)

В§12 P4+ chain end-to-end functional: codegen-side (hexa MIR вҶ’ PTX) and silicon-side (PTX вҶ’ ptxas вҶ’ RTX 5070 sm_120 driver-JIT вҶ’ numeric correctness) both **measured-PASS**. 25 PRs landed today including the **first three ever В§12 P4+ silicon-fire closures** (RFC 067 WMMA, RFC 068 f16, RFC 069 unroll byte-eq) + codegenвҶ”silicon reconcile (PR #193). `nvptx_lower_test` smoke: 9/9 вҶ’ 25/25 cases this session.

---

## 1 В· Completed (measured-PASS, landed on origin/main)

### 1a вҖ” codegen scaffolding (RFC 055 В§1-В§12 P3)

- [x] **RFC 055 Stage-1 scaffold** вҖ” NVPTX target enum, PTX opcode table, address-space constants, target enum dispatch
- [x] **RFC 055 055-P0** вҖ” PTX text emit pass for FP64-arithmetic subset (`add.f64`, `mul.f64`, `mov.f64`, `ret`, `.func`, `.reg .f64`)
- [x] **RFC 055 055-P1** вҖ” `@gpu_kernel` end-to-end vec-add slice (`.visible .entry`, `.param .u64`, `ld.global.f64`, `st.global.f64`, `mov.u32 %tid.x`, address arithmetic, bounds-check `setp + bra`)
- [x] **RFC 055 055-P2** вҖ” naive FP64 GEMM `@gpu_kernel` (i-j-k loop, FMA-ready)
- [x] **RFC 055 055-P3a** вҖ” `--target=nvptx64-nvidia-cuda-sm{80,90}` dispatch in `compiler/main.hexa`
- [x] **RFC 055 055-P3b** вҖ” per-Local PTX register-kind classification (`.f64` / `.u32` / `.u64` / `.pred`)
- [x] **RFC 055 055-P3b** вҖ” `STMT_BR` / `STMT_BR_COND` / `STMT_CALL gpu_*` / `STMT_LOAD` / `STMT_STORE` generic lowering
- [x] **RFC 055 055-P3c** вҖ” `@gpu_kernel` / `@gpu_device` partition (`gpu_kind` field on `MFunc`)
- [x] **RFC 055 055-P4** вҖ” `gpu_barrier()` block-wide sync (`bar.sync 0;`)
- [x] **RFC 055 055-P4+** вҖ” `gpu_atomic_add()` global `atom.add.f64`
- [x] **RFC 055 055-P4+** вҖ” `gpu_warp_shuffle()` `shfl.sync.idx.b32`
- [x] **RFC 055 055-P4+** вҖ” Tensor Core MMA scaffold (NVPTX_RKIND_FRAG, `_nvptx_wmma_mnemonic` table, STMT_CALL recognition)
- [x] **RFC 055 055-P4+** вҖ” mixed-precision scaffold (NVPTX_RKIND_F16/_BF16/_F32, classifier rules)
- [x] **RFC 055 055-P4+** вҖ” `_nvptx_unroll_pass` MVP (canonical 3-block back-edge, factor=2)

### 1f вҖ” Crash-recovery cycle (2026-05-21)

Recovery cycle after macOS crash lost two in-flight stash diffs (rounds 5-8 GPU.md doc + RFC 071 P2.1 spec, both unpushed). The original artifact directories referenced from those stashes (`rfc067_p9_rounds_5_7_2026_05_21/`, `rfc067_pA_round8_2026_05_21/`, `rfc067_p6_revalidate_2026_05_21/`) were lost system-wide. Stash patches preserved at `docs/notes/crash_recovery_2026_05_21/`. Re-fired the idempotent subset on ubu-2 RTX 5070 sm_120; new artifact: `archive/fires/rfc067_pB_crash_recovered_2026_05_21/`.

- [x] **F-RFC075-METAL-SUBDIV-NUMERIC-EQ** рҹӣё вҖ” vec-sub + vec-div MIR shapes silicon-validated on Apple M3 (cherry-pick `ca49aea1` from N2 sub-agent worktree, codegen now recognises **5 shapes**: vec-add + vec-mul + vec-sub + vec-div + vec-scale). `vec_sub` (3-buffer) **byte-eq** (max|О”|=0, byte_mismatch=0/1024). `vec_div` **вүӨ1 ULP** (max_ulp=1, 284/1024 cells deviate by вүӨ1 ULP) вҖ” Apple M3 GPU likely decomposes IEEE FP32 divide into `rcp + mul`, which is the standard GPU compromise (cuBLAS / Metal Performance Shaders both do this; not a codegen issue). Falsifier PASS criterion = byte-eq for arith with no decomposition + вүӨ4 ULP for divide. Artifact: `archive/fires/rfc075_metal_subdiv_2026_05_21/` (vec_sub.metal/.air/.metallib + vec_div.metal/.air/.metallib + host_subdiv.swift + result.json)
- [x] **F-RFC067-HGEMM-SCALEUP-HEXA (full 5-shape via shape-port)** вҖ” N4 sub-agent fired hand-emit PTX variants `wmma_{384,512,768,1024}x{...}_grid.ptx` produced by scaling the 256-shape's address-arithmetic constants + WMMA stride operands (microcode + 16-warp 4Г—4 block layout identical across all 5). Re-measured 5-shape ratios on ubu-2 RTX 5070 (200 timed launches per shape, 20 warmup, `cudaEventRecord` per-iter sync): **M=256 ratio 0.767** В· **M=384 ratio 0.740** В· **M=512 ratio 0.417** В· **M=768 ratio 0.350** В· **M=1024 ratio 0.287**. Hexa TFLOPS: 3.50 В· 9.67 В· 10.42 В· 16.69 В· 15.61. cuBLAS TFLOPS: 4.56 В· 13.06 В· 24.97 В· 47.66 В· 54.34. **Monotonic degradation** as M grows вҖ” naive K-loop is bandwidth-bound, lacks shared-memory tiling + software pipelining + async copies + split-K. Matches the optimiser-gap pattern documented in `reference_ptx_diff_perf_oracle` memory. M=256 ratio 0.767 matches commit `d9b737a2` (methodology stability across two fires). Artifact: `archive/fires/rfc067_pD_hgemm_followon_2026_05_21/` (host.c 440 lines + 4 new PTX + result.json). Honest scope: 4 new PTX are HAND-emit (not from compiler codegen); compiler `nvptx_target.hexa` still shape-locked at 256 вҖ” variable-M emission via the same compiler path is a follow-on (would benefit from RFC 071 P3 module-loader bridge to drive MIR вҶ’ PTX from source); no numeric correctness check at new shapes (timing only вҖ” shape-port preserves WMMA microcode so correctness inherits from M=256)

- [x] **F-RFC075-METAL-REDUCE-SUM-NUMERIC-EQ + CODEGEN INTEGRATION** рҹӣё вҖ” Apple M3 silicon-fire + codegen integration both landed. Silicon side: N=1024 input filled with `1.0`s, threadgroup=32 вҶ’ 32 per-SIMD-group outputs, all **exactly 32.0** (byte-eq, max|О”|=0.0, byte_mismatch=0/32). Hand-emit `reduce_sum.metal` uses Apple's `simd_sum` + lane-0 gated per-group write. Codegen side: N5-retry sub-agent commit `78b0e489` cherry-picked as `402ef897` вҖ” `compiler/codegen/metal_target.hexa` now recognises **6 shapes** (vec-add + vec-mul + vec-sub + vec-div + vec-scale + **reduce-sum** вҖ” the FIRST non-element-wise shape). New `_metal_mfunc_is_reduce_sum_shape` recogniser + `_metal_emit_reduce_kernel_signature` (2-buffer, NOT 3-buffer) + `_metal_emit_reduce_sum_body` (simd_sum + lane-0 gated `c[group_id] = v`). - [ ] **F-RFC067-HEXA-SGEMM-MMA-M16N8K32 (N90, ISA-LAYER FALSIFIED)** вҖ” **HARDWARE-ILLEGAL shape for FP16 multiplicands on all NVIDIA tensor-core generations through Blackwell sm_120**. ptxas rejects `mma.sync.aligned.m16n8k32.f32.f16.f16.f32` with `Illegal matrix shape '.m16n8k32' for instruction 'mma'` on **all 6 shapes / all arch targets (sm_90/90a/120/120a) / all ptxas versions (12.0.140, 12.9.86, driver-JIT 13000)**. Sanity cross-check with `m16n8k32.s32.s8.s8.s32` got DIFFERENT error (vector-size mismatch) вҶ’ confirms ptxas accepts `.m16n8k32` shape token, but only for sub-byte int types. **Root cause (PTX ISA 8.7 В§9.7.13.4.13)**: `m16n8k32` defined exclusively for sub-byte integer multiplicands (`.s8`/`.u8`/`.s4`/`.u4`/`.b1`). K-doubling comes from packing more sub-byte elements into same register footprint вҖ” **physically impossible for 2-byte FP16**. FP16 supported shapes only: `m8n8k4`, `m16n8k8`, `m16n8k16`. **Falsification more fundamental than target-bump** (task's honest-scope category): instruction simply doesn't exist for FP16 on any NVIDIA HW. **Peak TFLOPS N/A** (6/6 PTX load failures at driver-JIT, kernel never launched). cuBLAS re-measured 67.13 TFLOPS @ M=1536 (matches N77 baseline within variance). N77 36.06 / ratio 0.533 remains current `mma.sync`-path peak. **Path forward for "more arithmetic per mma issue on FP16"**: Hopper `wgmma.mma_async.sync.aligned` (sm_90+) or Blackwell `tcgen05.mma` (sm_100+) вҖ” different instruction classes (descriptor-based shared mem + async pipelining + different reg allocation). NOT a drop-in shape swap; multi-session refactor. Within `mma.sync` semantics, remaining levers: CTA output-tile (currently 64Г—64), pipeline depth (currently 2-slot DB), ldmatrix layout. Artifact: `archive/fires/rfc067_pT_hexa_sgemm_m16n8k32_2026_05_21/` (PTX pure-ASCII addressing math correct; only mma instruction itself ISA-illegal)

N199 is the full-kernel reproduction (m64n64k16 + Hilbert + conditional) confirming **wgmma = Hopper-only, consumer Blackwell needs tcgen05.mma (sm_100a B200) which RTX 5070 also lacks**. **cuBLAS catch-up progress = unmeasurable on sm_120**. Per N195: "16% gap on RTX 5070 CANNOT close via wgmma (cuBLAS itself uses Ampere mma.sync per N104 SASS-diff). Closure comes from mma.sync scheduling/tiling/occupancy, not wgmma." Full N199 kernel ready for H100/H200/GH200 hot-fire when Hopper pool appears. All 8 shapes (M=256..8192) PTX pure-ASCII, ptxas-PASS on sm_90a вҖ” strongest claim available infra supports. Combined with Round 25 synthesis: 4 closes (N195 wgmma impossible, N197 named-bar insufficient, N198 PPSH catastrophic, N199 wgmma+Hilbert blocked) + 1 win (N196 TMA available). Path forward on sm_120 = TMA mbarriers + named-bar + Hilbert + multi-stage cp.async combined (multi-cycle). Artifact: `archive/fires/rfc067_pwgmma_hilbert_conditional_2026_05_22/`

- [x] **рҹӣёрҹӣёрҹӣёрҹӣёрҹӣё F-RFC067-HEXA-TMA-SWIZZLE128 PASS (N204, 0.85 CEILING SHATTERED вҖ” peak 0.992 ratio)** вҖ” TMA descriptor with CU_TENSOR_MAP_SWIZZLE_128B + matched ldmatrix on ubu-1 RTX 5070 sm_120. **All 6 shapes bit-exact PASS** (maxabs=maxrel=0). **Per-shape (cuBLAS / hexa / ratio / vs N200-full)**: **M=512 23.43/23.24/0.992 (+33.7pp)** В· M=1024 51.07/48.42/**0.948** (+21.0pp) В· M=2048 66.25/63.25/**0.955** (+17.8pp) В· M=4096 69.37/67.42/**0.972** (+17.2pp) В· M=6144 70.17/68.21/**0.972** (+17.5pp) В· **M=8192 70.18/68.61/0.978 (+15.9pp)**. **0.85 CEILING SHATTERED at every shape**. **g3-honest confound**: SWIZZLE_128B requires TMA box innermost вүҘ128B вҶ’ forced widening K_TILE 16вҶ’64 (2048BвҶ’8192B/tile). Loaded `(row<<8)|col` pattern via TMA with each swizzle mode, dumped smem to discover mapping. **SWIZZLE_128B formula**: `byte_offset = m*128 + (atom_k XOR (m & 7)) * 16 + (k_fp16 % 8) * 2`. Matches CUTLASS Sw<3,4,3> algebra. nvcc `cuda::ptx::ldmatrix` + `cuda::ptx::cp_async_bulk_tensor` hit template-overload errors in CUDA 12.9 `mbarrier_try_wait_parity.h` вҖ” empirical probe more reliable. **Resources**: 66 regs/thd, 16400 B shmem/CTA. **One bring-up issue**: v1 fill (cyclic K-only `i%4`/`i%3`) made all C[m,n] expected=396 at K=6144. ### 1g вҖ” RFC 075 Metal P4 silicon-fire (2026-05-21) рҹӣё

First-ever Mac silicon-fire for hexa-lang. Crash-recovery cycle freed Mac-local capacity; Metal P4 closure was the next P4-ready row in В§10. MSL kernel text emitted via the same shape that `codegen_emit_metal_msl` produces (verified by reading `compiler/codegen/metal_target.hexa:318-350` `_metal_emit_preamble` + `_metal_emit_kernel_signature` + `_metal_emit_vec_add_body` constants), compiled through Apple's toolchain, dispatched on Apple M3 GPU, compared bit-exact to a CPU reference. Artifact: `archive/fires/rfc075_metal_p4_2026_05_21/`.

- [x] **F-RFC075-METAL-EMIT-PIPELINE** вҖ” `xcrun -sdk macosx metal -c vec_add.metal -o vec_add.air` rc=0 + `xcrun metallib vec_add.air -o vec_add.metallib` rc=0. AIR=3,584 B, metallib=3,741 B. Toolchain: Apple metal 32023.883 (metalfe-32023.883), target `air64-apple-darwin25.5.0`

- [x] **F-RFC075-METAL-NUMERIC-EQ** рҹӣё вҖ” N=1024 FP32 cells, LCG-deterministic inputs (`a[i] = lcg_f32()`, `b[i] = lcg_f32()`, ref `c[i] = a[i] + b[i]`), dispatch as 1D grid (`dispatchThreads(grid, threadsPerThreadgroup:1024)`), read-back via `MTLBuffer.contents()`. **max|О”|=0.0**, **byte_mismatch=0/1024** (bit-exact via `bitPattern` comparison). PASS

- [x] **F-RFC075-METAL-SCALEUP-NUMERIC-EQ** рҹӣё вҖ” 7-shape sweep NвҲҲ{1024, 4096, 16384, 65536, 262144, 1048576, 4194304}. ALL byte-eq with CPU reference (`max|О”|=0.0`, `byte_mismatch=0/N` per shape). Effective bandwidth scales with N: 0.05 вҶ’ 0.25 вҶ’ 1.08 вҶ’ 3.73 вҶ’ 12.19 вҶ’ 23.13 вҶ’ **50.53 GB/s** at N=4 M (3В·NВ·4 B / median_ms В· 1e9). Apple M3 LPDDR5 theoretical ~100-150 GB/s shared with CPU вҶ’ 35-50% efficiency at saturation. 50 timed launches per shape (5 warmup) using `cuLaunchKernel`-equivalent `MTLCommandBuffer.waitUntilCompleted` wall time. Artifact: `archive/fires/rfc075_metal_p4_scaleup_2026_05_21/`
- [x] **F-RFC075-METAL-ROOFLINE-PROBE** рҹӣё вҖ” Apple M3 GPU roofline probe via hand-emit `kernels.metal` with 5 kernels (1op / 4op / 16op / 64op / 256op chained per cell) Г— 4 shapes (N=64K/256K/1M/4M). 50 timed launches per (kernel, N). Crossover regime at N=4M: 1op = 34.91 GB/s + 2.91 GFLOPS (memory-bound) В· 16op = **52.37 GB/s peak + 69.83 GFLOPS** (bandwidth saturation) В· 64op = 48.73 GB/s + **259.87 GFLOPS peak** (compute-bound) В· 256op = 11.11 GB/s + 236.98 GFLOPS (register pressure or thermal). Apple M3 8-core GPU theoretical ~3.2 TFLOPS FP32 вҶ’ achieved 260 GFLOPS вүҲ 8 % (single-buffer, no SIMD-group optimization). Roofline crossover = between 16-op and 64-op for vec-add-style memory pattern. Artifact: `archive/fires/rfc075_metal_roofline_2026_05_21/`. Hand-emit kernels are NOT codegen-produced (probe is for Apple M3 characterisation, not codegen validation)

g3 caveats:
- Single vec-add kernel shape (the only shape `codegen_emit_metal_msl` recognises today); general `MFunc` вҶ’ MSL emit is multi-session follow-on
- USER-LOCAL Mac fire path: this kernel cannot run on ubu-2 x86_64 / RTX 5070 (the Mac and the Nvidia GPU lanes are now bi-platform validated and remain orthogonal)
- N=1024 (small); larger N + multi-threadgroup + reductions are follow-on cycles
- No perf measurement вҖ” silicon-fire correctness only; Metal vs cuBLAS / Metal Performance Shaders perf comparison is a separate cycle

### 1h вҖ” F-FUSION-ATTENTION-FLASH: fused attention moat (structural-formal + wall ruled-out) (2026-05-25)

The В§10 moat case cuBLAS structurally CANNOT do: a single fused flash-attention kernel computing `softmax(Q K^T/вҲҡd) V` with online-softmax tiling (running max + running sum), **never materializing the NГ—N score matrix S to HBM**. Hand-emit pure-ASCII PTX (`archive/fires/fusion_attention_flash_2026_05_25/flash_attn.ptx`), fired on ubu-2 RTX 5070 (sm_120, driver 580) against a cuBLAS-using baseline (`cublasGemmStridedBatchedEx` QK^T вҶ’ write S вҶ’ standalone softmax kernel вҶ’ `cublasGemmStridedBatchedEx` В·V). GPU uncontended at fire time (0% util, no compute procs вҶ’ timed wall taken, not deferred). **Verdict: рҹ”ө structural-formal + рҹ”ҙ wall axis ruled-out (g3 closed-negative вҖ” both terminal, both publishable).**

- [x] **F-FUSION-ATTENTION-FLASH structural (clause a)** рҹ”ө вҖ” PROVEN closed-form. fused **1 launch** vs baseline **3**; S-matrix HBM round-trip fused **0 B** vs baseline **4В·NВІВ·4 B** (O(NВІ) eliminated). Total-HBM ratio `R(N,d) = (5Nd+4NВІ)/(4Nd) = 1.25 + N/d` вҶ’ **9.25Г— @512, 17.25Г— @1024, 33.25Г— @2048, 65.25Г— @4096** (d=64). hexa-native compiled `ratio_check.hexa` reproduces R exactly (`4Г—R(2048,64)=133 вҮ’ 33.25`) вҶ’ **рҹ”ө SUPPORTED-FORMAL**. $0 structural oracle (`structural_oracle.c`, deterministic, no GPU) is the PRIMARY finding. Verdict: `.verdicts/fusion-attention-flash/F-FUSION-ATTENTION-FLASH.txt`
- [x] **F-FUSION-ATTENTION-FLASH ptxas-clean** вҖ” `flash_attn.ptx` pure-ASCII; `ptxas -arch=sm_80` rc=0, `-arch=sm_90` rc=0; driver-JIT load on sm_120 (`cuModuleLoadDataEx`, `CU_JIT_TARGET_FROM_CUCONTEXT`) rc=0
- [x] **F-FUSION-ATTENTION-FLASH-NUMERIC** вҖ” fused output vs **f64 CPU reference** rel-err вүӨ 1e-2 PASS at NвҲҲ{512,1024,2048,4096} d=64 (max_rel ~1e-6, three orders under tol). Baseline matches identically (validates the layout)
- [x] **F-FUSION-ATTENTION-FLASH wall (clause b) вҖ” рҹ”ҙ FALSIFIED (ruled-out axis)** вҖ” cudaEvent, 20 warmup + 200 timed, median ms. fused(1 launch) vs baseline(3 launch): **0.415 vs 0.282 @512 В· 0.823 vs 0.559 @1024 В· 1.640 vs 1.143 @2048 В· 3.788 vs 2.492 @4096**. The cuBLAS baseline is **1.4вҖ“1.5Г— FASTER at every shape**. The fused kernel is a naive 1-thread-per-query scalar online-softmax; cuBLAS runs QK^T and В·V on Tensor Cores. **Closed-negative: structural fusion ALONE does not win wall vs cuBLAS** вҖ” the moat (1 launch, 0 S-HBM) is necessary but NOT sufficient. The вүҘ30% wall additionally requires the fused inner GEMMs at Tensor-Core throughput (wmma m16n8k* tiling over Q/K/V blocks, S in shared memory). This deterministically scopes the next cycle.
- [ ] **В§10 box "Whole-program-fusion вүҘ30%" stays `[ ]`** вҖ” structural-only; the wall was measured and NOT won (g3 honesty вҖ” structural-only / closed-negative leaves the box open with the finding noted). В§5b "Attention scoring fusion" remains `[ ]` pending the Tensor-Core fused kernel.

g3 caveats:
- The wall negative is specific to the NAIVE scalar fused kernel вҖ” it does NOT falsify the moat thesis; it falsifies "fusion alone suffices" and pre-registers the Tensor-Core fused-attention kernel as the next falsifier
- d=64 single-head, FP32 throughout (the GEMMs are small enough that the O(NВІ) S round-trip the baseline pays is not large vs its TC GEMM speed); longer-context / multi-head / fp16 may shift the crossover and is a follow-on
- No LLVM (@F f1). No C-transpile changes (@F f2) вҖ” CPU codegen files MD5-identical pre/post (`self/runtime.c`, `compiler/codegen/{x86_64_linux,arm64_darwin}.hexa` unchanged); the fire is hand-emit PTX + .c hosts only

### 1h вҖ” Whole-program-fusion epilogue: GEMM + bias + GeLU structural finding (2026-05-25) рҹӣё

The classic fused-epilogue case cuBLAS cannot do: GEMM + bias-add + GeLU activation in one kernel. A single hexa-emit kernel computing `C = GeLU(A@B + bias)` fuses the GEMM, the bias-add, and the GeLU into one epilogue and writes the MГ—N result to HBM ONCE. This is a `$0`-oracle + ptxas-clean codegen round; the **timed silicon fire is DEFERRED to a serial follow-up** (ubu-2 is shared вҖ” parallel timed fires contend and poison wall numbers). Branch `gpu-fusion-epilogue` (from origin/main `49fcf884`). Artifact: `archive/fires/fusion_epilogue_gemm_bias_gelu_2026_05_25/`.

- [x] **F-FUSION-EPILOGUE-GEMM-BIAS-GELU (structural oracle, PRIMARY finding)** рҹ”ө вҖ” `$0` deterministic launch/byte count (`tool/fusion_epilogue_structural_oracle.hexa`, compiled hexa, run on ubu-1). At the LLaMA-7B FFN shape (M=4096 N=11008 K=4096; C tensor 180 355 072 B): **FUSED = 1 launch + 1Г— MГ—N HBM C-write** vs **BASELINE (cuBLAS-using stack: `cublasSgemm` вҶ’ bias-add kernel вҶ’ GeLU kernel) = 3 launches + 3Г— MГ—N HBM C-write**. **launch reduction 66.667 % AND HBM-write reduction 66.667 %** вҖ” both clear the вүҘ30 % whole-program-fusion gate by construction. Shape-independent (256Ві cross-check identical, since the C-write traffic depends only on MГ—N). Verdict persisted `.verdicts/fusion-epilogue-gemm-bias-gelu/fusion_epilogue_structural.txt`
- [x] **F-FUSION-EPILOGUE-PTXAS-CLEAN** рҹ”ө вҖ” `ptxas -arch=sm_80 fused_gemm_bias_gelu.ptx` on ubu-2 (CUDA 12.0): **RC=0, 23 registers, 0 spill, 4264-byte cubin**. PTX pure ASCII, md5 `1d7380556da101b7e37017b79eed6f01`. GeLU via tanh-approx (`ex2.approx.f32` base-2 exp + `rcp.approx.f32`), GEMM FP32 `fma.rn.f32`, bias-add + activation fused before the single `st.global.f32`
- [ ] **F-FUSION-EPILOGUE-WALL (timed advantage, DEFERRED-to-serial-follow-up)** вҖ” fused 1-launch kernel wall vs the 3-launch cuBLAS-using baseline wall on ubu-2 RTX 5070. Host launchers authored (`tool/fusion_epilogue_fused_host.c` 1-launch driver-API + `tool/fusion_epilogue_cublas_baseline.c` 3-launch cuBLAS stack, both rel-err вүӨ1e-2 vs f64 CPU ref). DEFERRED вҖ” shared host; this round is `$0`-oracle + ptxas-clean only. **GPU.md В§10 вүҘ30 % box stays `[ ]` until this timed wall lands** (the structural advantage is proven; the timed flip needs the wall)

g3 caveats:
- The structural oracle counts launches + HBM C-write bytes вҖ” a deterministic real measurement. It is NOT a timed wall; the timed perf advantage is the deferred follow-on
- The fused kernel is a one-thread-per-output naive GEMM (correctness + fusion-structure demonstration), not a WMMA-tiled perf kernel вҖ” the fusion *advantage* (1 vs 3 launches, 1Г— vs 3Г— HBM C-write) is independent of the inner GEMM tiling
- cuBLAS-LT *does* have a limited `GELU_BIAS` epilogue; the baseline models the canonical NN-stack path using plain `cublasSgemm`/`cublasGemmEx` (no fused epilogue), which is what flame/PyTorch-eager-class stacks emit
- No LLVM (@F f1), no C-transpile change (@F f2) вҖ” CPU codegen byte-identical pre/post (only doc + new artifact/tool files added)

### 1h вҖ” F-FUSION-LAUNCH-AMORT вҖ” launch-overhead amortization $0 oracle (2026-05-25) рҹӣё

The В§5f launch-overhead-amortization case made concrete + ptxas-clean. A single fused hexa-emitted kernel computes the **5-op elementwise chain `y = residual + scale * GeLU(a*x + b)`** (mul В· add В· gelu В· mul-by-scale В· add-residual) in ONE launch, with t1..t4 living in registers; a per-op baseline issues the SAME chain as **5 separate kernel launches**, each round-tripping the working tensor through HBM (eager-stack / per-op-library semantics). Pre-registered falsifier **F-FUSION-LAUNCH-AMORT**: the fused single-launch kernel beats the 5-launch baseline by вүҘ30% wall in the launch-bound regime. This cycle is the **$0 structural/projection oracle + ptxas-clean**; the timed silicon wall is DEFERRED-to-serial (ubu-2 shared). Artifact: `archive/fires/gpu_fusion_launch_amort_2026_05_25/`.

- [x] **F-FUSION-LAUNCH-AMORT structural advantage PROVEN ($0 oracle, exit 0)** рҹӣё вҖ” deterministic hexa-native oracle (`oracle.hexa`, built native, exit 0). **Launch count: fused 1 vs baseline 5 (5.0Г— fewer)**. **HBM traffic/elem: fused 2R+1W=3 vs baseline 6R+5W=11 (3.67Г— more for baseline)**. **Closed-form wall projection** from MEASURED per-launch overhead (В§1g F-RFC067-PB-TIMING, warm Nth-launch L=1 Вөs; conservative effective BW=200 GB/s): `wall_fused = L + RfВ·cВ·n`, `wall_baseline = 5L + RbВ·cВ·n`. Launch-bound (nвҶ’0): `pct_faster вҶ’ 1 вҲ’ 1/5 = 80%`. Bandwidth-bound (nвҶ’вҲһ): `pct_faster вҶ’ 1 вҲ’ Rf/Rb = 1 вҲ’ 3/11 = 72.7%`. **The 30%-crossover `n* = 2.5L/(cВ·(Rf вҲ’ 0.70В·Rb))` has `(Rf вҲ’ 0.70В·Rb) = (3 вҲ’ 7.7) = вҲ’4.7 < 0` вҮ’ n\* NEGATIVE вҮ’ no crossover вҮ’ the вүҘ30% advantage is UNCONDITIONAL across all n**. Sample curve: n=64 вҶ’ 79.98% В· n=1024 вҶ’ 79.69% В· n=65536 вҶ’ 74.6% В· n=1M вҶ’ 72.88%. **The falsifier is over-satisfied** вҖ” it predicted a launch-bound-only crossover, but the fused kernel wins on BOTH the launch axis (1<5) AND the HBM-traffic axis (3<11), so the вүҘ30% wall win never drops below 30%. Verdict verbatim: `.verdicts/fusion-launch-amort/fusion_launch_amort.txt`.
- [x] **ptxas-clean вҖ” `ptxas -arch=sm_80 -v` on ubu-2 (CUDA 12.0)** вҖ” both PTX modules assemble clean, 0 spill. **fused_chain.ptx rc=0** (11 regs, 392 B cmem[0], 0 spill). **baseline_chain.ptx rc=0** (5 entries k1_mul/k2_add/k3_gelu/k4_mul_scale/k5_add_resid = 10/10/11/10/12 regs, all 0 spill). Pure ASCII (driver-JIT ptxas rejects non-ASCII PTX comments). Log: `archive/fires/gpu_fusion_launch_amort_2026_05_25/ptxas_clean.log`. ptxas is not a timed run (no GPU contention).
- [x] **numeric correctness harness** вҖ” `host_fusion_launch.c` (cuLaunchKernel + cuEvent timing, `tool/r067_p4_host.c` pattern) compares the fused kernel to an f64 CPU reference of the identical chain (tanh-approx GeLU), tol 1e-2 abs (tanh.approx.f32 ~2вҒ»В№В№ rel bound). Numeric PASS confirmation is part of the DEFERRED timed fire.
- [x] **TIMED SILICON WALL вҖ” CONFIRMED 2026-05-25** рҹӣёрҹӣё вҖ” `host_fusion_launch.c` fired on ubu-2 RTX 5070 sm_120 (GPU 0% util pre-fire, uncontended, 20 warmup + 200 timed median) across nвҲҲ{1024, 16384, 262144, 4194304, 16777216}: fused beats the 5-launch baseline **73.1вҖ“76.2% wall UNCONDITIONALLY** вҖ” n=1024 74.1%/3.86Г— В· n=16384 73.1%/3.72Г— В· n=262144 76.2%/4.20Г— В· n=4194304 74.6%/3.93Г— В· n=16.7M 73.5%/3.77Г—, all вүҘ30% gate PASS, numeric max|О”|=1.1e-5 (abs) PASS. **The closed-form projection [72.7%,80%] is CONFIRMED BY MEASUREMENT** (рҹҹў SUPPORTED-NUMERICAL). **This FLIPS the В§10 "вүҘ30% whole-program fusion advantage" box to `[x]`** (domain @goal В· В§5f launch-overhead axis). Verdict verbatim: `.verdicts/fusion-launch-amort-wall/F-FUSION-LAUNCH-AMORT-WALL.txt`.

g3 caveats:
- The 80% / 72.7% figures are a closed-form PROJECTION from a measured per-launch constant (L=1 Вөs) + a model (memory-bound elementwise; per-op kernel = bandwidth-limited) вҖ” NOT a measured wall. The serial timed fire is the empirical confirmation.
- The HBM-traffic count (3 vs 11) is the structural ground truth; it is exact, not modeled. The launch-count (1 vs 5) is exact. The PROJECTION layer (translating those into a вүҘ30% wall) is what the timed fire validates.
- No LLVM (@F f1). No C-transpile change (@F f2). CPU codegen untouched.

### 1i вҖ” F-FUSION-ATTN-WMMA вҖ” Tensor-Core fused flash-attention codegen (round 2 of 3) (2026-05-25) рҹӣё

The Tensor-Core successor to the round-1 naive-scalar flash-attention kernel (В§13 / `archive/fires/fusion_attention_flash_2026_05_25/`), which lost its wall **1.4вҖ“1.5Г— slower** than cuBLAS because its inner QK^T and В·V GEMMs were scalar `fma` loops. This round re-authors the fused `softmax(QK^T/вҲҡd)В·V` kernel with **both inner GEMMs on Tensor Cores** via `wmma.mma.sync m16n16k16` (f16 mul, f32 acc), the **S tile resident in SHARED MEMORY (never to HBM)**, and online softmax (running max + sum) on the smem S tile. Pre-registered falsifier **F-FUSION-ATTN-WMMA-WALL**: clause (a) ptxas-clean + 1 launch + 0 S-HBM + Tensor-Core inner GEMMs; clause (b) [ROUND 3] beats cuBLAS-batched-TC-GEMM+softmax by вүҘ30% wall. **THIS round = codegen + ptxas-clean (3 arches) + $0 structural oracle (clause a); the timed wall (clause b) is DEFERRED-to-round-3** (parent runs timed fires serially вҖ” uncontended GPU). Artifact: `archive/fires/fusion_attention_wmma_2026_05_25/`.

- [x] **clause (a) вҖ” WMMA fused kernel EMITS + ptxas-clean (3 arches)** рҹӣё вҖ” hand-emit `flash_attn_wmma.ptx` (RFC 067 WMMA cookbook + `compiler/codegen/nvptx_target.hexa::_nvptx_wmma_mnemonic` emit family). Pure ASCII (0 non-ascii bytes). **ptxas `-arch=sm_80` rc=0** (48 regs, 5824 B smem, 0 spill, 392 B cmem) В· **ptxas `-arch=sm_90` rc=0** (48 regs, 5824 B smem, 0 spill) В· **driver-JIT `sm_120` rc=0** on the live RTX 5070 (`cuModuleLoadDataEx` + `CU_JIT_TARGET_FROM_CUCONTEXT`, entry `flash_attn_wmma` resolved 48 regs / 5824 B static smem вҖ” a LOAD probe, NO kernel launch, NO timing). **Footprint fits the RTX 5070 envelope** (В§1f caps): 48 regs вүӘ 65536/block, 5824 B smem = 11.8% of the 49152 B/block cap; S tile (1024 B) + O tile (4096 B) resident in smem.
- [x] **clause (a) вҖ” structural moat PRESERVED + Tensor-Core inner GEMMs confirmed** рҹӣё вҖ” `$0` compiled-hexa oracle (`structural_oracle.hexa`, `hexa build` + run вҖ” `hexa verify` g5 is broken on both ubu hosts, so compiled-hexa per the round protocol; stdout verbatim in verdict): **1 launch vs baseline 3**, **0 S-HBM vs baseline 4В·NВІВ·4 B** (67 108 864 B @ N=2048), total-HBM ratio `R(N,d)=1.25+N/d` reproduced (4Г—R(2048,64)=133). **Static PTX ground-truth grep**: `wmma.mma.sync` **Г—5 distinct** (1Г— `mma.row.col` QK^T + 4Г— `mma.row.row` PВ·V over d=64) **vs round-1 ZERO** вҖ” the round-1 wall-loss root cause (scalar inner GEMMs) is ADDRESSED. **`st.global` Г—1** вҖ” the ONLY HBM write is the final O; the S tile uses `wmma.store.d вҖҰshared.f32` exclusively вҮ’ **S never touches HBM**.
- [x] **clause (b) ROUND-3 harness READY (NOT run)** вҖ” `fa_wmma_host.c` (fused launcher: IEEE f16 in/out, f64 CPU reference on the f16-rounded inputs, rel-err вүӨ 1e-2, `cuEvent` 20 warmup + 200 timed median) + `fa_cublas_tc_baseline.c` (cuBLAS `CUBLAS_GEMM_DEFAULT_TENSOR_OP` 3-launch QK^T вҶ’ softmax kernel вҶ’ PВ·V, `cuEvent` timed). Both **`nvcc -c` compile-clean on ubu-2** (rc=0). Round-3 plan: serial uncontended fire at NвҲҲ{512,1024,2048,4096} d=64; win = `baseline_ms/fused_ms вүҘ 1.30`.

g3 caveats:
- **WALL clause (b) вҖ” ROUND-3 FIRED 2026-05-25: рҹ”ҙ FALSIFIED.** Timed on ubu-2 RTX 5070 (uncontended, GPU 0% pre-fire, 20 warmup + 200 timed median, d=64): the fused single-CTA wmma kernel is **9.4вҖ“15.5Г— SLOWER** than the cuBLAS-TC 3-launch baseline вҖ” N=512 0.157 vs 0.0166 ms (9.4Г—) В· N=1024 0.335 vs 0.0309 ms (10.8Г—) В· N=2048 0.819 vs 0.0617 ms (13.3Г—) В· N=4096 2.930 vs 0.189 ms (15.5Г—) вҖ” **AND numeric FAILs** (max_rel 2.6вҖ“4.8 > 1e-2 tol; max_abs ~3вҖ“6e-5). **Ruled-out axis (the round-3 finding):** Tensor-Core *instructions* alone do NOT win the wall. The round-2 kernel is **single-CTA** (S/P/O tiles + 48 regs resident in one block's smem) so it occupies **~1 of the RTX 5070's 48 SMs** while cuBLAS launches a grid of thousands of CTAs вҖ” the structural moat (1 launch, 0 S-HBM) is real but dominated by a 47/48-SMs-idle parallelism deficit. Beating cuBLAS attention requires cuBLAS-grade **multi-CTA work distribution + occupancy + tiling** (flash-attention's actual design: one CTA per (query-block, head)), not just `wmma.mma.sync`. The clause-(a) verdict (рҹ”ө codegen/structural) stands; clause (b) is a closed-negative. Verdict `.verdicts/fusion-attention-wmma-wall/F-FUSION-ATTN-WMMA-WALL.txt`.
- **В§10 box is NOT touched.** The "вүҘ30% whole-program fusion" box is already `[x]` (flipped via the В§5f launch-amortization axis, PR #1028). This GEMM-fusion (attention) axis needs its OWN round-3 timed Tensor-Core wall to win вҖ” flipping nothing here.
- The kernel keeps the S tile in shared memory and applies online softmax via a shared-mem round-trip of the S/O tiles (correct-by-construction, sidesteps the mma fragment laneвҶ’(row,col) layout) вҖ” a perf-relevant choice the round-3 fire measures; an in-fragment softmax is a follow-on optimization if the wall is close.
- No LLVM (@F f1). No C-transpile change (@F f2). `compiler/codegen/*.hexa` UNTOUCHED (hand-emit PTX); CPU codegen MD5 preserved (`x86_64_linux.hexa b50a2a3cвҖҰ`, `arm64_darwin.hexa b0a397dcвҖҰ`).

---

### 1j вҖ” F-FUSION-ATTN-MULTICTA вҖ” multi-CTA wide-KV fused flash-attention (round 4) (2026-05-25) рҹҹ 

The round-4 attack on the GEMM-fusion (attention) axis after round-3's рҹ”ҙ wall loss. Pre-registered falsifier **F-FUSION-ATTN-MULTICTA-WALL**: author a **CORRECT, multi-CTA** fused flash-attention kernel that saturates the SMs (keeping online softmax + S-in-shared-never-HBM + wmma inner GEMMs), then re-time vs cuBLAS-TC 3-launch вҖ” win = вүҘ30% faster (ratio вүӨ 0.70). **Result: рҹҹ  QUANTIFIED-PARTIAL** вҖ” a correct multi-CTA kernel that closes the gap ~3вҖ“8Г— but does **not** beat cuBLAS-TC. Artifact: `archive/fires/fusion_attention_multicta_2026_05_25/`.

- [x] **NUMERIC вҖ” round-3 "FAIL" was a METRIC ARTIFACT, kernel is CORRECT** рҹҹў вҖ” round 3's reported `max_rel 2.6вҖ“4.8 = FAIL` came from the naive `|err|/(|want|+1e-6)` metric exploding on the **many near-zero attention output elements** (|want| вүӘ 1e-6) вҖ” NOT a kernel bug. Under the honest **per-row-scaled + RMS** relative metric the round-3 *algorithm* is already correct, proven independently in clean CUDA-C `nvcuda::wmma` (rel_rowscale 5e-4, rms 2.6e-4, PASS). The shipped hand-PTX multi-CTA kernel `flash_attn_wmma_mcta` then PASSes numeric at all 4 shapes vs the f64 CPU ref: rel_rowscale **6.3e-4 / 5.6e-4 / 6.3e-4 / 7.1e-4** (N=512/1024/2048/4096), rms ~2.7e-4 вҖ” matching the CUDA-C oracle exactly (вҮ’ the hand-PTX WMMA fragment handling is correct).
- [x] **round-3 was ALSO already multi-CTA** вҖ” the round-3 grid was `N/16` CTAs (not single-CTA); the real deficit was **1 warp/CTA doing per-16-key serial online-softmax overhead**. The round-4 lever is **widening the KV tile from BK=16 to BK=256** (16 wmma key-subtiles per softmax round), amortizing the softmax+rescale overhead 16Г—.
- [x] **ptxas-clean (3 arches) + footprint** вҖ” pure ASCII (0 non-ascii bytes). **sm_80 rc=0** (41 regs, 28864 B smem, 0 spill, 392 B cmem) В· **sm_90 rc=0** (32 regs, 28864 B smem, 0 spill) В· **driver-JIT sm_120** loads + runs OK. 28864 B smem/CTA = **58.7% of the 49152 B/block cap (FITS)**; S(16Г—256)+O(16Г—64) resident in smem, never to HBM. **Grid occupancy:** `N/16` вҮ’ **32 / 64 / 128 / 256 CTAs** (vs 48 SMs) вҖ” max grid saturation (multi-warp-per-CTA was MEASURED slower: cuts grid count + raises smem/CTA).
- [x] **TIMED WALL (clause b) вҖ” рҹҹ  PARTIAL** вҖ” ubu-2 RTX 5070 (clean, 0% util, 0 compute procs, cuEvent 20 warmup + 200 timed median, d=64). Shipped **hand-PTX fused vs cuBLAS-TC**: N=512 0.0566 vs 0.0167 ms (**3.40Г—**) В· N=1024 0.114 vs 0.0308 ms (**3.70Г—**) В· N=2048 0.244 vs 0.0617 ms (**3.96Г—**) В· N=4096 0.954 vs 0.190 ms (**5.01Г—**). **Gap closure: round-3 9.4вҖ“15.5Г— вҶ’ round-4 3.4вҖ“5.0Г—.** The CUDA-C-validated geometry floor (nvcc-vectorized scalar loops) is even tighter: **1.32 / 1.44 / 1.65 / 2.04Г—** вҖ” the hand-PTX scalar softmax/rescale loops are un-vectorized (~2вҖ“2.5Г— slower than nvcc's `ld.shared.v4`/unroll), so a hexa-codegen path with vectorized smem loads could approach this floor.

g3 caveats:
- **NOT a win.** Fused is still **1.3вҖ“5.0Г— slower** than cuBLAS-TC (ratio > 0.70) вҖ” the вүҘ30% GEMM-fusion-axis win is **not achieved**. Honest tier = рҹҹ .
- **Binding constraint identified:** at d=64 the **per-16Г—16-tile online-softmax overhead вҖ” NOT S-HBM traffic вҖ” is the wall**. cuBLAS amortizes its GEMMs over huge tiles the tiny 16Г—16 WMMA fused path cannot match; wide-KV amortization narrows but does not close this. The structural moat (1 launch, 0 S-HBM) is real and preserved but not the bottleneck at this shape.
- **В§10 box is NOT touched** вҖ” stays `[x]` only via the launch-amort axis (PR #1028). The GEMM-fusion (attention) axis remains NOT-won.
- **No paper** вҖ” `paper_gate` forbids рҹҹ  partial sections; this is neither a вүҘ30% win nor a clean closed-negative (the kernel works, it just loses the wall).
- No LLVM (@F f1). No C-transpile change (@F f2). `compiler/codegen/*.hexa` UNTOUCHED (hand-emit PTX); the CUDA-C `.cu` files are correctness/geometry oracles only, not the shipped fused path. CPU codegen MD5 preserved.

### 1k вҖ” F-FUSION-ATTN-DECOMP вҖ” full dimensional-decomposition sweep В· KV-split hypothesis (round 5) (2026-05-25) рҹҹ вҶ’closed-neg

The round-5 attack: map the **complete parallel-decomposition space** of the fused `softmax(QK^T/вҲҡd)В·V` kernel vs cuBLAS-TC 3-launch, and specifically test whether the **KV-SPLIT (z-axis, flash-decoding)** dimension closes the small-N occupancy gap left by round-4 (N=512 grid = only 32 CTAs < 48 SMs). Pre-registered falsifier **F-FUSION-ATTN-DECOMP-WALL**. Swept **153 configs** = N{512,1024,2048,4096} Г— Bq{16,32,64} Г— kv_split{1,2,4,8,16} Г— BK{64,128,256}, d=64 вҖ” **all numeric PASS** (rel_rowscale вүӨ 1e-2 vs f64 CPU ref). Tool: a CUDA-C `nvcuda::wmma` **flash-decoding oracle** (2-kernel: partial-O + LSE-merge), authored correctly вҖ” `kv_split=1` reduces EXACTLY to the round-4 algorithm (max_abs 4.02796e-05 identical). **Result: рҹҹ  QUANTIFIED-PARTIAL вҶ’ closed-negative.** Artifact: `archive/fires/fusion_attention_decomp_2026_05_25/`; ledger `exports/sweep/gpu-attn-decomp-2026-05-25/`.

- [x] **KV-SPLIT CLOSES the small-N occupancy gap вҖ” user hypothesis CONFIRMED** рҹҹў вҖ” N=512 Bq16: occupancy **32 вҶ’ 128 CTAs** (kv=1вҶ’kv=4), wall **0.146 вҶ’ 0.058 ms** = **2.53Г— intra-framework speedup**, reaching **parity with the round-4 single-kernel** (0.0568 ms) despite the 2-pass partial-O+merge tax. The benefit **saturates** at the split K where ctas_partial вүҘ ~48 SMs (N=512 plateaus at kv=4=128 CTAs; **kv=8/16 REGRESS** via over-subscription + merge cost).
- [x] **KV-split is a SMALL-N-ONLY lever** вҖ” at NвүҘ2048 the grid is already saturated by `N/Bq` alone, so KV-split adds only the partial-O HBM round-trip tax (grows O(NВ·splitВ·d)): decomp-best **0.668 ms vs round-4 single-kernel 0.245 ms @ N=2048 (2.7Г— WORSE)**. Net-neutral at small N, net-negative at large N.
- [x] **BK=256 confirmed best** within every fixed (N,Bq,kv) (round-4 finding re-confirmed); **Bq>16 uniformly slower** (cuts grid, the opposite of what small-N needs).
- [x] **OPTIMUM PER SHAPE (vs cuBLAS-TC)** вҖ” N=512 Bq16/kv4/BK128 **3.47Г—** В· N=1024 Bq32/kv4/BK256 **5.88Г—** В· N=2048 Bq64/kv4/BK256 **10.82Г—** В· N=4096 Bq16/kv8/BK256 **13.17Г—**. Best overall = **3.47Г— @ N=512**.

g3 caveats:
- **NOT a win.** Best ratio 3.47Г— (> 0.70). The вүҘ30% GEMM-fusion-axis win is **not achieved** by any decomposition. Honest tier = рҹҹ .
- **Closed-negative on the decomposition axis:** *no dimensional decomposition of hand-PTX flash-attn beats cuBLAS-TC at d=64.* KV-split trades **occupancy вҶ” HBM-traffic** вҖ” it does not breach the round-4 binding constraint (per-16Г—16-tile online-softmax overhead vs cuBLAS huge-tile GEMM efficiency). The GEMM-tile-efficiency wall is **confirmed fundamental**.
- The 2-pass oracle's absolute walls carry a partial-O HBM round-trip + 2nd-launch tax the round-4 single-kernel avoids; the **decomposition trend** is isolated within the consistent 2-pass frame, with the round-4 single-kernel given as the absolute cross-reference.
- **В§10 box is NOT touched** вҖ” stays `[x]` via launch-amort only; GEMM-fusion (attention) axis remains NOT-won.
- **No paper.** Captured as a closed-negative finding in the discovery log + ledger; `paper_gate` not triggered (no вүҘ30% win; the closed-negative is a re-confirmation of the round-4 wall via a new axis, not a fresh disproof worth a paper scaffold).
- No LLVM (@F f1). No C-transpile change (@F f2). `compiler/codegen/*.hexa` UNTOUCHED (hand-emit PTX path); the CUDA-C `.cu` is a correctness/decomposition oracle only. CPU codegen MD5 preserved.

### 1m вҖ” F-FUSION-ATTN-ROOFLINE вҖ” N204 roofline-GEMM-toolkit transplant (round 7) (2026-05-25) рҹҹ вҶ’closed-neg

The round-7 attack: hexa ALREADY hits the GEMM roofline standalone (N204 "TMA SWIZZLE_128B" reached **cuBLAS 0.978 parity @ M=8192**, PRs #333/#335) вҖ” the round-4/5 fused attention lost its wall (best 3.47Г—) NOT because hexa can't do roofline GEMM, but because the fused kernel's inner QK^T and PВ·V GEMMs were naive (single-warp, 16Г—16 wmma tiles, no TMA, no double-buffer, no swizzle). This round transplants the proven N204 roofline toolkit (TMA `cp.async.bulk.tensor` + double-buffered K/V tiles + 64Г—64 large `mma.sync.m16n8k16` tiles + 4-warp 2Г—2 layout) into the fused `softmax(QK^T/вҲҡd)В·V` inner GEMMs and measures % of the cuBLAS-TC + theoretical roofline. Pre-registered falsifier **F-FUSION-ATTN-ROOFLINE**: ratio вүӨ 1.10 vs cuBLAS-TC on at least one shape (NвҲҲ{2048,4096}, d=64) AND report achieved % of the sm_120 FP16 tensor-core roofline. **Result: рҹҹ  INSUFFICIENT (target NOT hit) + closed-negative finding.** Artifact: `archive/fires/fusion_attention_roofline_2026_05_25/`.

- [x] **clause (a) вҖ” kernel emits + ptxas-clean** рҹӣё вҖ” hand-emit `flash_attn_tma_v2_{2048,4096}.ptx` (pure ASCII, 0 non-ascii bytes). **ptxas `-arch=sm_120a` rc=0** (68 regs, 0 spills, 1 barrier, 8 B stack). 5 `cp.async.bulk.tensor` (TMA) + 64 `mma.sync.aligned.m16n8k16` + 32 `ldmatrix` + 1 `st.global` (final O only вҖ” S NEVER to HBM, moat preserved). cuOccupancyMaxActiveBlocksPerMultiprocessor = **1 CTA/SM** (smem 99136 B vs optin/SM 102400 B).
- [x] **clause (b) вҖ” NUMERIC PASS via fa_mma_oracle.cu + silicon fire** рҹҹў вҖ” both shapes pass the honest per-row-scaled metric: N=2048 rel_rowscale 6.11e-4 / rms_rel 2.72e-4 В· N=4096 rel_rowscale 7.14e-4 / rms_rel 2.72e-4. Matches the round-4 oracle EXACTLY (max_abs 3.11e-5 @ N=4096 identical) вҶ’ algorithmic equivalence confirmed.
- [x] **рҹӣё MMA-FRAGMENT-MAP DISCOVERY** рҹҹў вҖ” the round-7 probe campaign (`probe2.cu` + `probe3.cu`) empirically established that **`mma.sync.m16n8k16 .trans` + `ldmatrix.x4` performs an 8Г—8-BLOCK transpose within each 16Г—16 fragment, NOT a full 16Г—16 transpose**. Non-trans + `mma.row.col` gives `C = AВ·B^T` (err 1e-7 MATCH). The PВ·V GEMM (contraction along V rows) therefore CANNOT use the same `.trans`-B path as QK^T; **v2 pre-transposes V into a separate smem buffer** so the proven non-trans path drives both GEMMs (probe3 err 6e-8 MATCH). Non-obvious empirical fact about m16n8k16 ldmatrix.x4 semantics not surfaced by PTX ISA narrative reading.
- [x] **рҹ”ҙ clause (c) вҖ” TIMED WALL ratio NOT вүӨ1.10** вҖ” fired on ubu-2 RTX 5070 sm_120, GPU 0% util, 0 compute procs (uncontended). 20 warmup + 200 timed cuEvent median:
  - **N=2048**: fused **0.324864 ms** / cuBLAS-TC **0.061568 ms** вҶ’ **ratio 5.276Г— SLOWER**. Fused 3.31 TFLOPS В· cuBLAS 17.44 TFLOPS.
  - **N=4096**: fused **1.281312 ms** / cuBLAS-TC **0.186624 ms** вҶ’ **ratio 6.866Г— SLOWER**. Fused 3.35 TFLOPS В· cuBLAS 23.01 TFLOPS.
- [x] **% OF ROOFLINE** (stated assumptions: sm_120 RTX 5070 from В§1f caps вҖ” 48 SM В· 2.542 GHz В· 192-bit bus):
  - **% of cuBLAS HGEMM achievable ceiling (~70.2 TFLOPS @ N204 M=8192)**: N=2048 **4.71%** В· N=4096 **4.77%**.
  - **% of theoretical FP16-TC peak (48 SM Г— 4 TC Г— 256 FMA Г— 2 FLOP Г— 2.542 GHz = 249.9 TFLOPS)**: N=2048 **1.32%** В· N=4096 **1.34%**.
  - cuBLAS-TC 3-launch attention reaches 17.4 / 23.0 TFLOPS = 24.8% / 32.8% of its own HGEMM ceiling вҖ” so cuBLAS's attention itself is ~3-4Г— off roofline.
- [x] **GAP-CLOSURE TRAJECTORY (final)** вҖ” round-3 9.4-15.5Г— вҶ’ round-4 3.4-5.0Г— вҶ’ round-5 3.47Г— вҶ’ **ROUND-7 5.3-6.9Г— (REGRESSION)**.
- [x] **OCCUPANCY ATTRIBUTION (direct measurement)** вҖ” `cuOccupancyMaxActiveBlocksPerMultiprocessor` on the real fn returned **1 CTA/SM** (smem-bound). At N=2048 grid=32 CTAs вҶ’ **only 32 of 48 SMs populated (66.7% SM coverage)**. At N=4096 grid=64 вҶ’ 48 SMs 1-CTA + 16 CTAs queued for serialized second wave. Round-4's BM=16 kernel had **8 CTAs/SM**; the 64Г—64 attention tile multiplies the resident-set smem 8Г— (Q + K[2] + V[2] + V^T[2] + S + P + O all simultaneously) вҶ’ occupancy collapse.
- [x] **DOUBLE-BUFFER ATTRIBUTION (paired-shape A/B)** вҖ” single-buffer occupancy-test variant (`flash_attn_tma_sb`, smem 74560 B, same 1 CTA/SM): wall 0.324896 ms. v2 double-buffer: 0.324864 ms. **О” 0.01% вҖ” double-buffer ZERO BENEFIT here**: kernel is occupancy-bound, not DMA-bound; the TMA overlap opportunity is unrealized (no parallel compute to hide loads behind at 1 CTA/SM, only 4 warps with mma chain that can't overlap its own smem dependencies on the same slot).

g3 caveats:
- **NOT a win.** Best ratio 5.27Г— (> 1.10 by 4.8Г—). Pre-registered target NOT hit. Honest tier = рҹҹ  INSUFFICIENT + closed-negative finding on the technique axis.
- **CLOSED-NEGATIVE (terminal):** *the N204 standalone-GEMM roofline toolkit DOES NOT TRANSPLANT to fused flash-attention.* The 64Г—64 tile that buys roofline-GEMM performance for a standalone GEMM COSTS attention occupancy because fused attention has fundamentally different smem residency (Q + K + V + V^T + S + P + O simultaneously resident вҖ” multiple O(BM Г— BK) and O(BM Г— d) tiles). The technique is correct in isolation (numeric PASS, ptxas-clean) but the architectural fit is wrong for this kernel. **Which N204 technique helped most: NONE moved the wall positively.** Rank by attribution: 64Г—64 tile (BACKFIRED, the main regressor) > TMA loads (NEUTRAL, save HBM but no occupancy to absorb) > double-buffer (ZERO) > swizzle (NOT APPLIED in v2 because the .trans-B path is invalid for PВ·V).
- **В§10 box is NOT touched** вҖ” stays `[x]` via launch-amort only; GEMM-fusion (attention) axis remains NOT-won.
- **No paper.** ORANGE INSUFFICIENT + re-confirmation of an already-CLOSED-NEGATIVE wall via a new failed-axis вҖ” `paper_gate` forbids per project.tape `paper_significance`.
- **Next-round wedge (recommendation):** shallower tile BM=32 (or BM=16 with multi-warp) + REGISTER-RESIDENT O (acc in registers, not smem) + selective TMA to restore вүҘ2-4 CTAs/SM occupancy WITHOUT abandoning TMA loads. Smem budget then ~34-50 KB вҶ’ 2 CTAs/SM, doubling occupancy.
- No LLVM (@F f1). No C-transpile change (@F f2). `compiler/codegen/*.hexa` UNTOUCHED (hand-emit PTX path); `.cu`/`.c` are oracle/host only. CPU codegen MD5 preserved.

### 1l вҖ” F-FUSION-AXISA-BREADTH вҖ” whole-program-fusion moat across the NN elementwise/norm surface (2026-05-25) рҹӣёрҹӣё

Broadens the В§10 moat (already `[x]` via the launch-amort wall, В§1h / PR #1028) from ONE workload to the **NN elementwise/reduction surface**: LayerNorm В· RMSNorm В· Softmax В· SwiGLU. Each = a fused 1-kernel vs an eager multi-launch baseline, timed on ubu-2 RTX 5070 sm_120 (uncontended 0% util, 20 warmup + 200 timed median), numeric vs an f64 CPU reference using the **HONEST per-row-scaled RMS rel metric** (tol 1e-2 вҖ” avoids the round-3 attention near-zero false-FAIL). Pre-registered falsifier per workload: fused (1 launch) beats eager by вүҘ30% wall. `hexa verify` (g5) is BROKEN on both ubu hosts вҖ” correctness settled via the compiled f64-ref harness, stdout persisted verbatim.

- [x] **LayerNorm** рҹҹў вҖ” eager 4-launch {reduce-mean, reduce-var, normalize, affine} вҶ’ fused 1; launch 4Г—, HBM 6вҶ’3. **large 4096Г—4096 = 66.2%** (fused 0.232 ms vs eager 0.687 ms, 2.96Г—) В· **small 256Г—512 = 72.7%** (3.67Г—). numeric rel вүӨ 1.5e-7. Verdict `.verdicts/fusion-axisA-layernorm/`.
- [x] **RMSNorm (LLaMA)** рҹҹў вҖ” eager 3-launch {reduce-sq, normalize, scale} вҶ’ fused 1; launch 3Г—, HBM 5вҶ’3. **large = 59.5%** (0.232 vs 0.573 ms, 2.47Г—) В· **small = 58.6%** (2.41Г—). numeric rel вүӨ 1.4e-7. Verdict `.verdicts/fusion-axisA-rmsnorm/`.
- [x] **Softmax (online)** рҹҹў вҖ” eager 4-launch {row-max, exp, row-sum, div} вҶ’ fused 1; launch 4Г—, HBM 6вҶ’4. **large = 65.9%** (0.238 vs 0.698 ms, 2.93Г—) В· **small = 56.3%** (2.29Г—). numeric rel вүӨ 1.9e-7 (HONEST per-row RMS вҖ” softmax probs go near zero). Verdict `.verdicts/fusion-axisA-softmax/`.
- [x] **SwiGLU** рҹҹў вҖ” eager 3-launch {sigmoid, mul-gate, mul-up} вҶ’ fused 1; launch 3Г—, HBM 8вҶ’3 (largest traffic cut вҖ” eager materialises s and t in HBM). **large n=16.78M = 63.0%** (0.334 vs 0.903 ms, 2.70Г—) В· **small n=131072 = 47.8%** (1.92Г—). numeric rel вүӨ 3.4e-7. Verdict `.verdicts/fusion-axisA-swiglu/`.

**4/4 workloads PASS вүҘ30% in BOTH launch-bound and bandwidth-bound regimes (8/8 measurements, 8/8 numeric).** The moat is now a robust GENERAL result across **N+1 = 5 workloads** (these 4 + launch-amort 73вҖ“76%), not a single data point. cuBLAS/cuDNN supply tuned GEMMs but the elementwise/norm/activation glue is exactly what fusion owns. All ptxas modules `-arch=sm_90 -v` clean, 0 spill. Ledger `exports/sweep/gpu-axisA-breadth-2026-05-25/`; artifact `archive/fires/fusion_axisA_breadth_2026_05_25/`. No LLVM (@F f1). No C-transpile change (@F f2). CPU codegen untouched (hand-emit PTX, pure ASCII).

### 1n вҖ” Axis E вҖ” autoregressive single-token fusion (LLM decode) вҖ” round 8 of N В· structural + projection (2026-05-25) рҹӣёрҹӣёрҹӣё

Novel axis E (sibling to axes A/B/C/D), declared post-axis-C. Fuses an entire transformer-decoder layer step at autoregressive batch=1 (post-first-token) decode into **2 mega-kernels per layer** (`decode_attn_fused` + `decode_ffn_fused`) so the q-vector flows through registers/smem across all 17+ logical ops (LN В· 3-GEMV Q/K/V В· KV-append В· QK В· softmax В· PV В· O-proj В· residual В· LN В· FFN-up В· SiLU В· FFN-down В· residual). The MOAT: at decode batch=1 the per-op compute is tiny (~5 Вөs) vs the per-launch overhead (~1 Вөs warm Г— 17 launches = 17 Вөs in eager), so launch-count reduction transfers almost 1:1 into wall reduction. This is the В§5f / В§5a axis extended to a full transformer layer's worth of ops вҖ” the regime where vLLM / PyTorch eager per-token decode bleeds the most.

**Shape**: GPT-2-small d=768, n_heads=12, head_dim=64, kv_cache_len L=512 (representative mid-context decode step).

- [x] **F-FUSION-AUTOREGRESSIVE-DECODE structural** рҹ”ө SUPPORTED-FORMAL вҖ” `$0` deterministic oracle (compiled hexa `oracle.hexa`, exit 0): per layer per token **fused 2 launches vs eager 17 (8.5Г— fewer)**; **temp-HBM round-trip 0 B vs 112 656 B (100% eliminated)**; closed-form launch-bound wall projection from MEASURED L=1 Вөs/launch warm overhead (`F-RFC067-PB-TIMING`) gives **70.6%** wall reduction (eager 17 Вөs vs fused max(5 Вөs, 2 Вөs)=5 Вөs); compute-saturated floor **вүҘ30%** unconditional (the 9 elementwise/norm/residual eager launches collapse into 0 in fused, ~9 Вөs overhead saved no matter what). For a 12-layer model: fused **24 launches/token vs eager 204** (8.5Г— fewer); fused **0 vs eager ~1.35 MiB temp-HBM/token**.
- [x] **ptxas-clean** вҖ” sm_80 + sm_90 RC=0 on both fused (2 mega-kernels: 32+27 regs В· 40 960+16 384 B smem В· 0 spill) and eager (17 entries: 8вҖ“26 regs each В· 0 spill). sm_120 reached via `cuModuleLoadDataEx` driver-JIT (forward-compat, same path as `F-FUSION-LAUNCH-AMORT` / `F-FUSION-ATTN-WMMA`). Smem 40 960 B fits the 49 152 B/block sm_80/sm_90 envelope.
- [x] **F-FUSION-AUTOREGRESSIVE-DECODE-WALL (round-9 timed silicon, FIRED 2026-05-26) вҖ” рҹ”ҙ FALSIFIED** вҖ” host harness (`tool/r9_walls/ar_host.c`) + f64 CPU reference + per-row-scaled rel вүӨ 1e-2 + NaN/Inf hard-fail; cuEvent 20 warmup / 200 timed median on ubu-2 RTX 5070 sm_120 (0% util pre-fire each L). Sweep L вҲҲ {64,256,512,1024,2048}. **NUMERIC FAIL both fused (max_relвүҲ1.61) and eager (max_relвүҲ1.9)** вҖ” the merged `decode_attn_fused` omits real online-softmax (uses `inv_sqrt_hd` placeholder weight + un-zeroed smem-atomic RMSNorm), and eager `k1_rmsnorm` is placeholder unit-scale + `k9_softmax` has no max-subtract/normalise (both PTX are R8 STRUCTURAL STUBS, not numerically-complete). **WALL: fused FLAT ~80 ms вҲҖL vs eager ~1.89вҶ’1.98 ms вҶ’ fused ~40-42Г— SLOWER at EVERY L** (pct_above_eager вҲ’4138 %@L=64 вҶ’ вҲ’3957 %@L=2048). **NO launch-bound win, NO crossover** вҖ” the projected 70.6 % does NOT materialise. ROOT CAUSE: `decode_attn_fused` is ONE CTA of 768 threads (single SM вүҲ 1/48 GPU, O(dВІ) per-thread QKV GEMV, serial smem-atomic RMSNorm); the 17 tiny eager kernels @ ~0.11 ms total ~1.9 ms still beat one 80 ms mega-kernel вҖ” the binding constraint is intra-kernel single-CTA serialisation, NOT launch count. The R8 structural moat (2 vs 17 launches, 8.5Г—; 100 % temp-HBM elim) is REAL but does NOT convert. Verdict `.verdicts/fusion-autoregressive-decode/F-FUSION-AUTOREGRESSIVE-DECODE-TIMED.txt`.
- [ ] **В§10 axis-E row** вҖ” closure lane (NOT a scoreboard slot; closure remains 8/8 вң…). **Round-9 outcome: structural вң… / timed wall рҹ”ҙ FALSIFIED** (fused ~40-42Г— slower вҲҖL; no crossover). Axis-E stays NOT-won вҖ” a fused-decode timed win needs real online-softmax + multi-CTA/warp-parallel tiled GEMVs inside the mega-kernels (single-CTA scalar inner GEMVs lose, same root cause as axis-B `F-FUSION-ATTN-WMMA` / axis-C `F-FUSION-LAYERBLOCK`).

Verdict `.verdicts/fusion-autoregressive-decode/F-FUSION-AUTOREGRESSIVE-DECODE.txt`; discovery `.discoveries/fusion-autoregressive-decode.tape`; CLAIMS.tape `@C fusion_autoregressive_decode_structural`; artifact `archive/fires/fusion_autoregressive_decode_2026_05_25/` (fused_decode.ptx + eager_decode.ptx + oracle.hexa + oracle_output.txt + ptxas_clean.log + FIRE.md). No LLVM (@F f1). No C-transpile change (@F f2). CPU codegen untouched (hand-emit PTX, pure ASCII).

**Verdict framing**: "structural launches per token per layer: hexa **2** vs eager **17** вҖ” vLLM / PyTorch API per-call structure forbids the fusion; projected launch-bound wall вүҘ**70%** above eager per-token (round-9 timed will confirm)."

---

## 2 В· Next layer (concrete, scope-bounded вҖ” pick one to start)

### 2a вҖ” Source-to-silicon e2e closure (RFC 068 last gap)

Today's silicon fires used hand-emit PTX (codegen verification via `nvptx_lower_test` smoke; silicon via fire). The remaining gap: a `.hexa` source file with `@gpu_kernel fn f16_vadd(...)` lowering through HIR вҶ’ MIR вҶ’ codegen_emit_ptx_sm80 вҶ’ ptxas вҶ’ fire.

- [ ] **source kernel fixture** вҖ” write `test/rfc068_f16_vadd_e2e.hexa` with `@gpu_kernel fn f16_vadd(a: [f16], b: [f16], c: [f16], n: i64)` body
- [ ] **HIR вҶ’ MIR lowering** вҖ” verify `let t: f16 = a[i] + b[i]` lowers to `STMT_LOAD .f16 + STMT_BINOP add_f16 + STMT_STORE .f16` with precision tag propagated
- [ ] **MFunc.gpu_kind = KERNEL** вҖ” `@gpu_kernel` annotation parse + lowering hooked
- [ ] **codegen emits launchable PTX** вҖ” `.visible .entry` + `.param .u64` quartet (a/b/c/n) + body
- [ ] **ptxas-clean check** вҖ” emitted PTX passes `ptxas -arch=sm_80`
- [ ] **fire on ubu-2** вҖ” driver-JIT + cuLaunchKernel + compare to f64 reference
- [ ] **`F-RFC068-E2E-NUMERIC-EQ`** PASS вҖ” full source-to-silicon chain byte-eq closure
- [ ] **commit** вҖ” same `archive/fires/` pattern as PR #189

### 2a finding (2026-05-20): build pipeline gap analysis

The blocker is NOT in `self/main.hexa::cmd_build` `--target=` validation
(adding a `nvptx64-*` branch there is one-line edit). The substantive
gap is the BUILD PIPELINE itself:

```
Current `hexa build` (CPU targets):
  src.hexa вҶ’ module_loader (flatten) вҶ’ hexa_v2 transpiler (.c)
           вҶ’ clang/zig cc вҶ’ native binary

Required for NVPTX:
  src.hexa вҶ’ module_loader (flatten) вҶ’ in-hexa compiler self-host
           вҶ’ MIR вҶ’ codegen_emit_ptx_sm80 вҶ’ PTX text
```

`hexa_v2` is the **bootstrap transpiler** that emits C вҖ” it doesn't
know about NVPTX. The NVPTX codegen lives in `compiler/codegen/
nvptx_target.hexa` and is invoked only from within the in-hexa
self-host pipeline (which today produces CPU artifacts via the
existing `compiler/*` tree, not via `hexa_v2`).

To wire `hexa build --target=nvptx64-*` properly, options are:
- (A) **Internal emit-driver pattern** вҖ” `cmd_build` synthesizes a
  small driver `import src.hexa + compiler/codegen/nvptx_target.hexa`
  and prints `codegen_emit_ptx_sm80(...)`. Substantial: requires
  exposing the full compiler pipeline as a callable.
- (B) **Compiler self-host on NVPTX** вҖ” the in-hexa compiler IS
  the build path for `--target=nvptx64`. Aligned with north-star в‘Ў
  (self-host already PROVEN for CPU at fixpoint per memory
  `project_compiler_native_self_host_fixpoint`); extending to
  NVPTX is the natural next step.
- (C) **Out-of-band emit driver** вҖ” keep using the external script
  pattern from PR #82 (`tool/dispatch_*.sh`). Today's 8 fires
  successfully demonstrate this works. **No `hexa build` wiring
  required** for the actual silicon-validation path.

Choice for this session: **(C)** вҖ” defer (A)/(B) as multi-session
campaigns. The В§1 ledger shows all silicon-fires landed via the
out-of-band pattern; full source-to-silicon `hexa build --target=
nvptx64-*` is a strategic infrastructure cycle for a separate
session.

**Update 2026-05-20 (RFC 071 P0 scaffold landed):** This gap is now
formally tracked as RFC 071 вҖ” see
`docs/rfc/rfc_drafts_2026_05_20/rfc_071_source_to_silicon_e2e.md`. P0
landed the `cmd_build` target-string recognition for
`nvptx64-nvidia-cuda-sm80` / `sm90` / `sm120` (informative deferred
exit + RFC pointer; CPU codegen path byte-identical, no LLVM, no new
C-transpile architecture per `@F f1`/`@F f2`). P1-P4 (real dispatch +
emit-driver module + module_loader bridge + e2e silicon fire) are
explicitly deferred multi-cycle work governed by the F-RFC071-* falsifier
battery. Approach **A (internal emit-driver synthesis)** is the
recommended P1-P2 path; **B (compiler self-host on NVPTX)** is the
P3+ convergence path once north-star в‘Ў's CPU self-host campaign
default-flips. Approach C remains the codegen-author fast iteration
shell вҖ” RFC 071 introduces a new path, not a replacement.

**Update 2026-05-20 (RFC 071 P1+P2 landed):** P1 replaced the
deferred-print + exit(1) branch with a call to
`self/main.hexa::_build_nvptx_emit_driver(src, sm_arch)` (F-RFC071-
TARGET-ACCEPT PASS). P2 added the spec sibling module
`compiler/cli/build_nvptx.hexa` defining
`pub fn build_nvptx_emit_driver(src_path, sm_arch) -> int` with a
canned stub PTX writer (`.version 7.0` / `.target sm_NN` /
`.address_size 64` / `.visible .entry _hexa_smoke() { ret; }`) вҖ”
F-RFC071-EMIT-DRIVER-INVOKE PASS as a STUB. **Honest punt (@D g3):**
the body emits CANNED PTX вҖ” F-RFC071-MODULE-LOADER-BRIDGE is
INTENTIONALLY deferred until P2.1 wires `codegen_emit_ptx_sm80(mir)`
(parse вҶ’ check вҶ’ lower вҶ’ codegen chain documented in the module
docstring). CPU codegen byte-identical (`F-RFC055-CPU-CODEGEN-
UNTOUCHED` PASS by md5; @F f1/@F f2 honored). В§10 box `[ ] В§12 P4+
source-to-silicon e2e` stays `[ ]` per @D g3 вҖ” only the P4 numeric-eq
falsifier flips it.

### 2b вҖ” Multi-tile WMMA GEMM K-loop (RFC 067 В§3 P4 spec form)

PR #191 closed the *single-tile* WMMA fire. The RFC 067 В§3 P4 spec asks for 64Г—64 GEMM = 4Г—4 output tiles Г— 4 K-tiles = 64 `wmma.mma` calls with `.shared` staging.

- [ ] **multi-tile kernel** вҖ” hand-emit `wmma_64x64.ptx` with explicit 4Г—4Г—4 nested loops
- [ ] **`.shared` staging slot allocation** вҖ” 4 KB shared mem for A/B double-buffer tiles
- [ ] **K-loop accumulator carry** вҖ” C fragment reuse across K-tile iterations (no spill)
- [ ] **host launcher** вҖ” `tool/r067_p4_multi_host.c` mirrors `r067_p4_host.c` but 64Г—64
- [ ] **fire on ubu-2 + compare to FP32 reference** вҖ” `вүӨ 1e-2 rel error` tolerance (the canonical f16-mul-f32-acc bound)
- [ ] **`F-RFC067-TILE-LOOP-NUMERIC-MULTI`** PASS
- [ ] **codegen-side hexa equivalent** вҖ” synthesize MFunc with multi-block K-loop body + multi-`gpu_wmma_mma` STMT_CALL emit

### 2c вҖ” Codegen-side BF16 silicon reconcile

Today's PR #193 reconciled `f16 вҶ’ b16` storage; bf16 reg type still trips ptxas 12.0 `.reg .bf16` parse.

- [ ] **PTX 7.8 toolchain bump probe** вҖ” test bf16 acceptance on `.version 8.0` / `.version 8.x` PTX targets
- [ ] **`add.bf16` instruction support** вҖ” verify ptxas accepts the bf16 arithmetic path
- [ ] **hexa codegen flip** вҖ” if PTX 8.x parses cleanly, emit `.version 8.0` + native `.reg .bf16` decl; else stay with `.reg .b16` and use bitcast
- [ ] **bf16 vec-add fire** вҖ” same pattern as PR #189 but bf16 inputs
- [ ] **`F-RFC068-NUMERIC-EQ-BF16`** PASS

### 2d вҖ” Hexa-native dispatch (replace direct-bash + sidesetep HEXA_FIRST_WARN)

PR #189/#190/#191 fires used direct one-shot bash; sustained automation needs hexa-native.

- [x] **stdlib/cloud dispatch primer** вҖ” `tool/dispatch_gpu_fire.hexa` orchestrates the whole fire (upload вҶ’ nvcc вҶ’ fire вҶ’ pull) through `stdlib/cloud` `cloud_copy_to_opts` / `cloud_exec_opts` / `cloud_copy_from_opts`. All shell-out rides `exec_capture` (codegen-wired) inside the cloud module вҖ” NOT `exec_argv` (no codegen branch вҶ’ would fail to link). f1/f2 preserved (no codegen touched).
- [x] **`tool/dispatch_gpu_fire.hexa`** вҖ” generic hexa-native fire dispatcher. Args `<host.c> <ptx>[,<ptx>...] [target-host]` + `--out/--remote/--result/--port/--insecure/--kernel`. Multi-PTX (comma-sep, argv-order). **Parses rc=0** (`hexa parse`) AND **compiles+links clean** (`hexa build` вҶ’ runnable arm64 binary, only harmless `runtime.h` comment warnings).
- [x] **smoke verify** вҖ” re-fired the RFC 055-P2 vec-add + naive-GEMM PTX (the kernels backing `dispatch_r055_p2_gemm.sh`) via the new dispatcher on ubu-2 RTX 5070. **result.json byte-identical to the recorded `state/rfc055_p2_2026_05_20/result.json`** (md5 `cd249eeb7879031e8fee53994d01e475` both sides) вҖ” all 4 falsifiers PASS, vec-add max|О”|=0 mismatches=0/1024, GEMM max|О”|=0 mismatches=0/4096. fire.log falsifier lines identical. $0.
- [x] **migrate** вҖ” `tool/dispatch_r055_p2_gemm.sh` removed (`git rm`); the hexa dispatcher re-fires the same kernels at measured byte-eq. Invoke: `dispatch_gpu_fire tool/r055_p2_host.c <vec_add.ptx>,<gemm.ptx> ubu-2`.

### 2e вҖ” `cp.async` pipelining (sm_80+) вҖ” performance, not correctness

- [ ] **PTX opcode constants** вҖ” `PTX_OP_CP_ASYNC_F16`, `PTX_OP_CP_ASYNC_COMMIT_GROUP`, `PTX_OP_CP_ASYNC_WAIT_GROUP`
- [ ] **codegen seam** вҖ” when WMMA kernel's K-loop body references `.shared` storage, emit `cp.async.cg.shared.global` for prefetch
- [ ] **double-buffer pattern** вҖ” two `.shared` staging slots; alternating fill/use
- [ ] **fire vs no-`cp.async` baseline** вҖ” same numeric output, measure throughput gain
- [ ] **`F-RFC067-CP-ASYNC-PERF`** вҖ” throughput delta documented (вүҘ 1.3Г— target)

## 3 В· Mid-term (deferred, scoped but multi-cycle)

### 3a вҖ” Additional dtypes

- [ ] **bf16 full silicon validation** (depends on 2c)
- [ ] **tf32 support** вҖ” `mma.sync.aligned.row.col.m16n16k8.f32.tf32.tf32.f32` for fp32 acceleration
- [ ] **int8 / int4** вҖ” quantization-friendly types; `dp4a` / `dp2a` instructions
- [x] **fp8 e4m3 / e5m2** (Hopper sm_90+) вҖ” codegen scaffold landed (RFC 068 В§3): `NVPTX_RKIND_F8_E4M3` / `_F8_E5M2` constants + `%fe3<id>` / `%fe5<id>` reg banks (silicon-canonical `.b8` container per PTX ISA В§5.4.1 + В§9.7.13.5) + classifier short-circuit on `.f8_e4m3` / `.f8_e5m2` precision tag + `ld.global.b8` / `st.global.b8` ld/st dispatch + Case 26/27 lower_test (ld/st round-trip, bank-isolation negative guard). **No silicon fire** вҖ” fp8 WMMA mnemonic family (`wmma.mma.sync...e4m3.e4m3.f32`) + sub-byte ABI (kernel-arg packing, addr alignment) + parser-side `@f8_*` named-type grammar are follow-on cycles.
- [ ] **posit** вҖ” custom dtype emission (lattice-friendly arithmetic; experimental)
- [ ] **MXFP4 / NVFP4** вҖ” Blackwell sm_120+ dtypes if applicable to RTX 5070

### 3b вҖ” Tensor Core families beyond canonical

- [ ] **bf16Г—bf16вҶ’f32** family вҖ” flip `_nvptx_wmma_mnemonic_family` selector
- [ ] **f16Г—f16вҶ’f16** family вҖ” accumulation in `.f16` (lower precision)
- [ ] **tf32Г—tf32вҶ’f32** (Ampere+) вҖ” TF32 default precision GEMM
- [ ] **fp8 wgmma** (Hopper sm_90+) вҖ” `wgmma.mma_async` (asynchronous warp-group)
- [ ] **wgmma 64x64x16, 64x128x16** large tiles вҖ” larger working tile geometry
- [ ] **m8n8k16 / m16n8k8** non-standard shapes вҖ” flexible mnemonic table

### 3c вҖ” Memory hierarchy + addressing

- [ ] **`.shared` register-tiling helpers** вҖ” auto-staging on `gpu_*` op patterns
- [ ] **`.local` scratch space** вҖ” register-spill destination for large kernels
- [ ] **`.const` constant bank** вҖ” for kernel-invariant LUTs
- [ ] **`ld.cs` / `ld.lu` cache hints** вҖ” streaming / last-use semantics
- [ ] **TMA (Tensor Memory Accelerator) sm_90+** вҖ” `cp.async.bulk.tensor.<dim>d.shared.global`
- [ ] **Async barriers** вҖ” `mbarrier.init`, `mbarrier.arrive`, `mbarrier.wait`

### 3d вҖ” Optimization passes

- [ ] **Unroll factor>4 with register-pressure analysis** вҖ” refuse factor=N if predicted register count > 64
- [ ] **Loop-carried dependency analysis** вҖ” true LCD detection (currently trusts user)
- [ ] **Loop fusion** вҖ” adjacent kernels with shared address вҶ’ single launch
- [ ] **Software pipelining** вҖ” interleave K-loop iterations
- [ ] **Constant folding through PTX** вҖ” known-constant operands вҶ’ immediate
- [ ] **Dead-code elimination** вҖ” operations whose results are never read
- [ ] **Register allocation** вҖ” proper graph coloring (currently 1:1 LocalвҶ’reg)
- [ ] **Polyhedral / affine loop transformation** вҖ” far-future advanced opt

### 3e вҖ” Source-level features (`@gpu_kernel` ergonomics)

- [ ] **`@gpu_kernel` attribute parse** вҖ” currently honored at lowering; verify parser surface
- [ ] **`@shared` annotation** вҖ” declare a `let` as shared-memory-resident
- [ ] **`@warp_intrinsic` annotation** вҖ” opt-in warp-shuffle intrinsics
- [ ] **`gpu_launch` builtin** вҖ” host-side `gpu_launch<<<grid, block>>>(kernel, args...)` lowering
- [ ] **`gpu_launch_async` / `gpu_event`** вҖ” CUDA stream + event API equivalents
- [ ] **`gpu_sync()` host-side** вҖ” `cudaDeviceSynchronize` wrapper
- [ ] **Source-level `gpu_atomic_*` family** вҖ” atomic ops covering add/cas/exch/min/max
- [ ] **Source-level `gpu_block_*` reductions** вҖ” sum / max / argmax via `bar.sync` + shared

### 3f вҖ” Multi-vendor (downstream вҖ” orthogonal to NVPTX)

- [ ] **HIP/AMD ROCm backend** вҖ” `gfx*` target dispatch (RFC 075 P0 scaffold landed: `compiler/codegen/rocm_target.hexa` + `rocm_lower_test.hexa` вҖ” emit stub returns `""`, P1+ multi-session BLOCKED вҖ” no AMD GPU in pool, cycle cannot silicon-fire-validate)
- [x] **Metal Performance Shaders** рҹӣё вҖ” Apple Silicon GPU (`@gpu_kernel` вҶ’ MSL source text; RFC 075 P1+P2+P3 codegen-only LANDED 2026-05-20 Campaign C: `compiler/codegen/metal_target.hexa` emits full MSL vec-add kernel source `kernel void vec_add(device const float* a [[buffer(0)]], ..., uint i [[thread_position_in_grid]]) { c[i] = a[i] + b[i]; }` for vec-add-shaped MIR; F-RFC075-METAL-EMIT-VEC-ADD PASS via 15-substring smoke `metal_lower_test.hexa`; **P4 silicon-fire LANDED 2026-05-21** вҖ” `xcrun -sdk macosx metal` + `metallib` + Swift `MTLComputePipelineState` dispatch on Apple M3 GPU. N=1024 FP32 vec-add max|О”|=0.0 byte_mismatch=0/1024. F-RFC075-METAL-NUMERIC-EQ PASS. Artifact: `archive/fires/rfc075_metal_p4_2026_05_21/`)
- [ ] **Intel oneAPI / Level Zero / SPIR-V** вҖ” Intel iGPU / Xe substrate (deferred to follow-on RFC, see RFC 075 В§2)
- [ ] **WebGPU / SPIR-V** вҖ” browser substrate
- [ ] **Cross-vendor abstraction layer** вҖ” shared IR pre-target

## 4 В· Performance benchmarking + competitive positioning

### 4a вҖ” Throughput baselines (vs vendor)

- [ ] **HGEMM throughput** вҖ” hexa-emit vs cuBLAS HGEMM on identical (M,N,K)
- [ ] **SGEMM throughput** вҖ” hexa-emit vs cuBLAS SGEMM
- [ ] **FP64 GEMM** вҖ” hexa-emit vs cuBLAS DGEMM
- [ ] **vec-add bandwidth** вҖ” hexa-emit vs CUDA stream `cudaMemcpy` (memory-bound)
- [ ] **kernel-launch overhead** вҖ” hexa-emit vs CUDA driver native (microseconds)

### 4b вҖ” End-to-end workload (flame integration)

- [x] **flame d=768В·12L transformer 1 step wall** вҖ” hexa-emit (forge) **20-43% faster** vs PyTorch eager (memory: `project_flame_phase4d9_closure`, commit `28e9d648`)
- [ ] **flame d=4096 LLaMA-3 8B inference latency** вҖ” single-token autoregressive
- [ ] **flame mixture-of-experts dispatch** вҖ” sparse expert routing on GPU
- [ ] **flame flash-attention 2 fused kernel** вҖ” vs `xformers.ops.memory_efficient_attention`

### 4c вҖ” vs alternative GPU compiler stacks

- [ ] **vs Triton** вҖ” same kernels in hexa vs Triton DSL
- [ ] **vs Mojo** вҖ” heavy GPU kernels in hexa vs Mojo MAX
- [ ] **vs Halide-GPU** вҖ” algorithm + schedule split comparison
- [ ] **vs ThunderKittens** вҖ” single-file abstraction over wmma
- [ ] **vs CUTLASS** вҖ” template-based GEMM library

### 4d вҖ” vs cuBLAS-using stacks (where hexa structural advantage applies)

- [ ] **PyTorch eager (uses cuBLAS+cuDNN+ATen)** вҖ” already partially measured (flame 4-D-9 closure)
- [ ] **JAX (XLA-based; uses cuBLAS via XLA)** вҖ” comparable architecture, more aggressive fusion
- [ ] **TensorFlow eager** вҖ” older but still widely deployed
- [ ] **MLX (Apple ML)** вҖ” Metal-based stack on M-series
- [ ] **TinyGrad** вҖ” minimalist Python-based codegen

---

## 5 В· Niches where hexa structurally beats cuBLAS (potential moat)

### 5a вҖ” Fusion that cuBLAS can't do

- [ ] **GEMM + epilogue fusion** вҖ” GEMM + bias_add + ReLU + dropout in single kernel (cuBLAS-LT does some, but limited). **STRUCTURAL FINDING 2026-05-25** (`F-FUSION-EPILOGUE-GEMM-BIAS-GELU`): fused `GeLU(A@B + bias)` hexa-emit kernel proven (by `$0` deterministic oracle, compiled hexa) to use **1 launch + 1Г— MГ—N HBM C-write** vs cuBLAS-using stack **3 + 3Г—** = **66.667 % reduction in BOTH launch-count AND HBM-write-traffic** at LLaMA-7B FFN shape (M=4096 N=11008 K=4096); PTX ptxas-clean sm_80 (RC=0, 0 spill). рҹ”ө structural-formal. Timed wall DEFERRED to serial follow-up. Artifact: `archive/fires/fusion_epilogue_gemm_bias_gelu_2026_05_25/`
- [ ] **Attention scoring fusion** вҖ” Q@K^T + softmax + V@ in single kernel (flash-attn pattern)
- [ ] **MoE dispatch + GEMM + reduce** вҖ” single kernel from gate to output
- [ ] **LayerNorm + GEMM fusion** вҖ” pre-layer-norm fused with GEMM weights
- [ ] **AdamW step fusion** вҖ” optimizer + parameter update fused with gradient compute

### 5b вҖ” Compile-time specialization

- [ ] **Static shape specialization** вҖ” known-(M,N,K) kernels avoid all runtime branches
- [ ] **Dead-output elimination** вҖ” masked outputs / pruned channels removed at compile time
- [ ] **Sparsity-pattern specialization** вҖ” block-sparse / structured-sparse layouts as compile-time facts
- [ ] **Mixed-precision auto-selection** вҖ” picker chooses dtype per layer based on compile-time error analysis

### 5c вҖ” Custom dtypes / non-IEEE arithmetic

- [ ] **n=6 lattice primitives** вҖ” RFC 057 / hexa-arch chip вҖ” non-binary lattice math on GPU
- [ ] **Posit arithmetic** вҖ” variable-precision posit emit
- [ ] **Interval arithmetic** вҖ” error-bounded compute
- [ ] **Stochastic rounding** вҖ” quantization-friendly random rounding

### 5d вҖ” Whole-program autograd-aware

- [x] **flame `ag_tape` / `ag_derive`** вҖ” already SD1-SD6 landed (PRs in main history)
- [ ] **GPU kernel fusion across autograd boundaries** вҖ” forward + backward kernels fused
- [ ] **Compile-time gradient symbolic simplification** вҖ” vs PyTorch's autograd runtime tape

### 5e вҖ” Non-NVIDIA hardware

- [ ] **Apple M-series Metal Performance Shaders** вҖ” Apple-silicon GPUs (currently flame uses CPU on M-series)
- [ ] **AMD MI300 / MI350** вҖ” ROCm HIP backend
- [ ] **Intel Xe / Arc** вҖ” oneAPI / Level Zero
- [ ] **Multi-vendor unified kernel** вҖ” same `@gpu_kernel` lowered to multiple backends

### 5f вҖ” Launch-overhead amortization (PyTorch eager / library-call stacks lose here)

- [x] **flame d=768В·12L transformer вҖ” 20-43% faster than PyTorch eager** вҖ” already measured (`project_flame_phase4d9_closure`). PyTorch eager pays per-op kernel launch overhead; cuBLAS calls cost вүҘ5 Ојs each. Hexa whole-program fusion eliminates the per-op launch path
- [x] **F-FUSION-LAUNCH-AMORT вҖ” fused 5-op chain $0 oracle + ptxas-clean (2026-05-25, В§1h)** рҹӣё вҖ” isolated launch-amortization case: fused `y = residual + scaleВ·GeLU(aВ·x+b)` (mulВ·addВ·geluВ·mul-scaleВ·add-resid) in **1 launch / 3 HBM transfers per elem** vs per-op baseline **5 launches / 11 transfers**. Deterministic oracle (exit 0) + closed-form projection from measured L=1 Вөs (В§1g): launch-bound 80%, bandwidth-bound 72.7%, **вүҘ30% UNCONDITIONAL across all n** (30%-crossover n\* negative). ptxas-clean sm_80 both modules (0 spill). Timed silicon wall DEFERRED-to-serial. Artifact: `archive/fires/gpu_fusion_launch_amort_2026_05_25/`
- [ ] **No PyBind11 / no ATen dispatch overhead** вҖ” cuBLAS via PyTorch goes through Python вҶ’ C++ Tensor вҶ’ ATen вҶ’ CUDA stream вҶ’ cuBLAS handle. Hexa-emit directly compiled into the binary
- [ ] **Static kernel selection** вҖ” cuBLAS-LT runtime heuristic picks an algorithm; hexa compile-time selects + bakes the algorithm
- [ ] **Single-shot binary** вҖ” no shared library boundary, no `cudaGetSymbolAddress`, no driver-level dispatch table

### 5g вҖ” Operator-specific surgical override

- [ ] **Replace one kernel mid-pipeline** вҖ” cuBLAS is monolithic API; hexa codegen lets a single GEMM in a chain be hand-tuned while the rest of the pipeline stays unchanged
- [ ] **Per-call-site precision** вҖ” same logical GEMM compiled with different precision per call site (cuBLAS forces uniform-handle precision)
- [ ] **Mixed-precision in single kernel** вҖ” f16 A Г— f16 B вҶ’ f32 accum вҶ’ bf16 store, all in one kernel; cuBLAS API forces handle-uniform dtype
- [ ] **Custom layout / striding** вҖ” cuBLAS has limited stride options; hexa per-kernel custom layouts (e.g., interleaved tile arrangements)

### 5h вҖ” Compile-time error / safety analysis

- [ ] **Static overflow check** вҖ” known input ranges + arithmetic chain вҶ’ compile-time overflow risk warning (cuBLAS = runtime only, often silent)
- [ ] **Compile-time NaN-Inf propagation reasoning** вҖ” track which operations could introduce NaN/Inf based on input domain analysis
- [ ] **Numerical-stability lint** вҖ” flag patterns like `large - small` that lose precision; cuBLAS users have no static signal
- [ ] **Determinism-mode at compile-time** вҖ” `@deterministic` annotation switches to deterministic-reduction emit at codegen; cuBLAS's `CUBLAS_PEDANTIC_MATH` is a runtime flag that costs perf

### 5i вҖ” Source-level visibility + ergonomics

- [ ] **`.so` blob vs source emit** вҖ” cuBLAS is closed-source binary; hexa users see + modify the emit path. Bug-fix loop: cuBLAS = file ticket + wait; hexa = patch source + rebuild
- [ ] **`hexa gpu disasm`** вҖ” view exact SASS via `cuobjdump`; cuBLAS too but harder to correlate to user code (the high-level mapping is lost in the closed binary)
- [ ] **Single-language stack** вҖ” host + device + autograd all in hexa-lang; cuBLAS-using stacks need Python/C++/CUDA polyglot
- [ ] **No vendor-lock-in path** вҖ” hexa codegen targets backend-agnostic IR; cuBLAS hard-binds to NVIDIA

### 5j вҖ” Algorithmic flexibility (cuBLAS = limited operator surface)

- [ ] **FlashAttention-style fused softmax + attention** вҖ” already a paper-derived pattern; cuBLAS doesn't cover the attention-block pattern directly (xformers / FlashAttention лі„лҸ„ library)
- [ ] **Online softmax** вҖ” single-pass numerically stable softmax (cuBLAS = no softmax at all)
- [ ] **Block-sparse / structured-sparse GEMM** вҖ” cuBLAS = dense only (sparse is cuSPARSE лі„лҸ„)
- [ ] **Custom reductions** вҖ” cuBLAS has SUM/MAX; arbitrary reduction (LogSumExp / soft-argmax) hand-written
- [ ] **Top-k / argmax fused with GEMM** вҖ” cuBLAS = GEMM only; hexa can fuse arbitrary epilogue

### 5k вҖ” Domain-specific kernel libraries (whole-program co-design)

- [x] **flame `ag_*` autograd-aware GEMM family** вҖ” SD1-SD10 vjp registry landed; GEMM kernels know about gradients (memory: `project_flame_mk2_cycle_2026_05_19`)
- [ ] **sim_universe lattice GEMM** вҖ” non-binary lattice arithmetic on GPU (RFC 057 bridge)
- [ ] **quantum amplitude-update kernels** вҖ” `stdlib/quantum` state-vector simulation (cuBLAS = no amplitude ops)
- [ ] **flame layer-fused training kernel** вҖ” forward + backward + AdamW + grad-clip in single kernel emit
- [ ] **NN-specific HEXA primitives** вҖ” `softmax`, `layer_norm`, `RoPE`, `swiglu` as first-class compiler-aware ops

### 5l вҖ” Edge / embedded / standalone deployment

- [ ] **Standalone cubin embed** вҖ” `hexa build` produces a binary with embedded `.cubin`; no separate cuBLAS .so dependency
- [ ] **AOT compilation** вҖ” kernel compiled once at build time; no runtime cuBLAS JIT
- [ ] **Multi-arch fat binary** вҖ” embed PTX for sm_70 + sm_80 + sm_90 in one cubin via hexa codegen
- [ ] **NVIDIA-runtime-free deployment** вҖ” minimal driver-only deployment surface (no cuBLAS/cuDNN required)
- [ ] **Containerized cubin** вҖ” single-binary container without `libcublas.so.12` dependency

### 5m вҖ” Measured wins to-date (g3-honest claims)

- [x] **flame d=768В·12L 1-step wall**: hexa-emit 191-268s vs PyTorch-eager 336.85s = **20-43% faster** (commit `28e9d648`, memory `project_flame_phase4d9_closure`)
- [x] **cp.async pipelining ~7% slower than no-async at K=64**: honest negative perf measurement (PR #207) вҖ” proves the codegen path works + sets the boundary where cp.async overhead amortizes (large K)
- [x] **WMMA + multi-warp grid + multi-K-tile + cp.async + tf32**: 5 distinct WMMA-family kernel patterns all silicon-validated max\|О”\|=0 vs FP32 reference (PRs #191/#205/#206/#207/#213)
- [x] **HGEMM throughput vs cuBLAS at M=N=K=256**: hexa-emit **4.0960 TFLOPS** vs cuBLAS GemmEx **8.1907 TFLOPS** = **ratio 0.500 Вұ0.0002** (6-run variance, sub-0.1% std). Closure criterion "вүҘ 50% of cuBLAS HGEMM" **MET at this shape** (PR #214). Caveat (g3): single shape; at larger M/N/K cuBLAS's k-loop unroll + ILP + shared-memory pipelining advantages compound; this single data point does NOT generalize. Multi-tile cp.async (PR #207) not yet integrated into this perf kernel вҖ” natural next-cycle.
- [ ] **HGEMM at M=N=KвүҘ1024**: pending вҖ” scale-up + cp.async integration to test if 0.50Г— ratio holds or degrades at large shapes (where cuBLAS optimizations matter)
- [x] **PyTorch eager d=1024 12L FP32 PROXY baseline on RTX 5070**: median 1-step wall = **116.286 ms** (std 0.104 ms = 0.089 % of median; peak 5,060 MiB) at d=1024 n_layer=12 batch=2 seq=512 FP32 Adam eager. RFC 072 P1 (this PR). Caveat (g3): this is the L4 ladder rung вҖ” RFC 072 В§2 spec (d=2048+ 12L) **does not fit** the 12 GB consumer-GPU envelope on PyTorch eager (50,257-token embed+head alone occupies ~5 GiB Adam-state overhead); d=4096 24L full-spec baseline requires H100 80GB multi-session. F-RFC072-WALL-PT-PROXY MEASURED В· F-RFC072-WALL-PT-FULL DEFERRED.
- [ ] **Whole-program-fusion вүҘ 30% over cuBLAS-using stack on a representative LLM workload** вҖ” sustained across model variants (flame d=768 partially measured)

---

## 6 В· Verification + safety

### 6a вҖ” Numerical

- [ ] **Bit-exact reference** вҖ” every emitted kernel compared to a bit-exact reference (cpu)
- [ ] **ULP-bounded checker** вҖ” tolerance-aware compare via a small test harness
- [ ] **Determinism mode** вҖ” force deterministic reductions (no atomics, ordered K-loop)
- [ ] **Kahan summation in GEMM K-loop** вҖ” error-bounded accumulator
- [ ] **NaN / Inf propagation** вҖ” verified across f16 / bf16 underflow / overflow

### 6b вҖ” Formal / semantic

- [ ] **PTX emit semantic equivalence proof** вҖ” Coq/Lean proof that codegen preserves MIR semantics
- [ ] **Register allocation correctness** вҖ” formal proof that allocation never aliases live ranges
- [ ] **Loop-unroll preservation** вҖ” proof that unrolled CFG вүЎ original CFG semantically

### 6c вҖ” Runtime safety

- [ ] **Bounds-check elision** вҖ” verified safe when guarded
- [ ] **Race-detection** вҖ” static analyzer over shared-memory accesses
- [ ] **Memory-ordering** вҖ” `bar.sync` / `mbarrier` placement audit

---

## 8 В· Far-future / research questions

### 8a вҖ” Beyond NVPTX

- [ ] **PTX вҶ’ SASS direct emit** вҖ” bypass ptxas, hand-emit GPU machine code
- [ ] **SPIR-V emit** вҖ” open-standard GPU IR
- [ ] **MLIR integration** вҖ” bridge to upstream MLIR (controversial вҖ” vs hexa-native principle)
- [ ] **Cooperative groups API** вҖ” multi-block synchronization

### 8b вҖ” Auto-tuning

- [ ] **Search-based tile-size selection** вҖ” autotune over block/grid/unroll
- [ ] **ML-based scheduling** вҖ” neural-net cost model for codegen choices
- [ ] **Random restart for kernel synthesis** вҖ” try N variants, pick best

### 8c вҖ” Specialized hardware

- [ ] **NVIDIA Grace-Hopper** вҖ” CPU+GPU unified memory (`MemcpyDtoH` becomes a no-op)
- [ ] **NVLink / NVSwitch** вҖ” multi-GPU collective primitives
- [ ] **AMD Instinct MI300A** вҖ” APU-style hexa kernel
- [ ] **Intel Ponte Vecchio** вҖ” Xe Matrix Extensions

### 8d вҖ” Esoteric / experimental

- [ ] **Quantum GPU bridge** вҖ” `stdlib/quantum` + GPU acceleration for state-vector simulation
- [ ] **Lattice n=6 GPU emit** вҖ” RFC 057 hexa-arch substrate, but on GPU
- [ ] **Neuromorphic compatibility** вҖ” `stdlib/sim_universe` substrate on GPU
- [ ] **Reversible computing primitives** вҖ” `gpu_uncompute` for memory-efficient autograd
